Along with portfolio and wealth management, SwissBorg also supports crypto trading, aggregating the lowest fees from many of the leading exchanges.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Swiss_Borg_Thematics_review_b0a96e9069.jpg"" alt=""SwissBorg Thematics review.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_review_b0a96e9069.jpg 237w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_review_b0a96e9069.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_review_b0a96e9069.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_review_b0a96e9069.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Image via <a href=""https://swissborg.com/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">SwissBorg</a></figcaption></figure><p>If you’re interested to know more about SwissBorg, including all the features + pros and cons, you can check out our <a href=""/review/swissborg-chsb/"">full SwissBorg review</a>.</p><h3>History and Vision</h3><p>Cyrus Fazel and Anthony Lesoismier-Geniaux co-founded SwissBorg in 2017. In a post on Medium, Fazel describes how his experience in the world of traditional finance armed him with the knowledge that helped bring SwissBorg into existence.</p><blockquote><p>“Blockchain would enable us to have the maximum reach and accessibility we required where Tokens would enable us to create any tailor-made investment mandate with no cost and intermediaries. And on top of this, we could leverage a strong community with decentralization based on a trusted meritocratic system.” (<a href=""https://medium.com/swissborg/meet-cyrus-fazel-swissborg-ceo-db07bbf50e90"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Source</a>)</p></blockquote><p>SwissBorg aims to give individuals complete control over their portfolios and investments. Today, the company sits at the crossroads of blockchain technology and personal finance.&nbsp;</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Swiss_Borg_values_d359c53832.jpg"" alt=""SwissBorg values.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Swiss_Borg_values_d359c53832.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Swiss_Borg_values_d359c53832.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Swiss_Borg_values_d359c53832.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Swiss_Borg_values_d359c53832.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Transparency, Equality Through Aeritocracy and Impartiality Are Among SwissBorg's Values. Image via SwissBorg</figcaption></figure><p>From its Auto-Invest feature to the more recent Thematics offerings, SwissBorg has transformed into a powerful crypto investment solution aimed at generating wealth.</p><h3>Products and Services</h3><p>Here are some of the key features of SwissBorg:</p><ul><li><strong>Wealth management:</strong> SwissBorg's wealth management app allows users to track and manage their crypto portfolios.</li><li><strong>Smart Engine:</strong> The brains behind the SwissBorg app! As you’re aware, market volatility often leads to price differences across exchanges. Smart Engine allows users to exchange between different fiat and crypto assets in the app. It scours multiple exchanges to ensure you get the best price.</li><li><strong>Native token:</strong> CHSB is SwissBorg’s native token that’s built on Ethereum. It gives holders voting rights to steer SwissBorg’s direction, unlocks higher loyalty tier benefits, and can be staked.</li><li><strong>SwissBorg Earn:</strong> This allows you to earn daily yield through staking or DeFi exposure. Depending on the asset you choose, you will have multiple strategies available: A conservative strategy with lower yields or a more aggressive strategy with higher returns. All profits earned are reinvested, which will compound your returns over time.</li><li><strong>Auto-Invest:</strong> Put investing on autopilot! This feature uses Dollar Cost Averaging (DCA), a popular strategy among investors, to reduce volatility by investing a fixed amount at regular intervals. You can auto-invest from any supported fiat or cryptocurrency to any cryptocurrency or Thematics, and you have full control over how much and how often you’d like to contribute.</li><li><strong>Asset analysis:</strong> Thanks to artificial intelligence, you can view full asset analysis for all cryptos available in the SwissBorg app. This is made achievable through CyBorg Predictor — which forecasts an asset's movement over the next 24 hours — and SwissBorg Indicator — which does technical analysis trend prediction. Community sentiment is also taken into account.</li><li><strong>Portfolio visualizer:</strong> This free tool provides in-depth investment analysis and statistics in an easy-to-understand format.<br>&nbsp;</li></ul><h3>SwissBorg Security</h3><p>Losing the private keys to your crypto wallet is a nightmare scenario. To address this, SwissBorg partnered with Fireblocks, which helps financial institutions protect digital assets from theft or hackers by using multi-party computation (MPC) and patent-pending chip isolation technology to secure private keys and API credentials.</p><p>MPC is the ability for multiple parties to jointly perform mathematical computations without one party ever revealing its secret to others. Fireblocks combines MPC-CMP with hardware isolation to create a multi-layer security technology. This eliminates a single point of failure and insulates digital assets from cyber-attacks, internal collusion, and human error.</p><h2>Thematics Overview</h2><p>SwissBorg offers multiple products that look to help crypto investors manage their wealth and offers a plethora of crypto investment avenues. Its Thematics offering is a pretty unique and innovative investment product in the industry.</p><h3>Concept and Rationale</h3><p>Crypto investment products are all the rage these days, and the top among those are exchange-traded funds. However, some of these ETFs don’t give you exposure to the full flavour of the industry. For example, <a href=""https://etfs.ark-funds.com/hubfs/1_Download_Files_ETF_Website/Fact_Sheets/ARKW_Factssheet.pdf "" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">ARK Next Generation Internet ETF</a>'s top-10 holdings do not include any individual crypto tokens. In fact, you’ll find names like car maker Tesla, e-commerce platform Shopify and games company Roblox. The only crypto-related exposure it has is through the Grayscale Bitcoin Trust, which rounds out the ETF's top 3 holdings.</p><p>This is where SwissBorg Thematics differs. Instead of doing away with crypto altogether, it exposes you directly to various tokens. It's important to note that Thematics are not ETFs.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Swiss_Borg_Thematics_homepage_2695bd3930.jpg"" alt=""SwissBorg Thematics homepage.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_homepage_2695bd3930.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_homepage_2695bd3930.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_homepage_2695bd3930.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_homepage_2695bd3930.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Thematics is SwissBorg's Most Advanced Investment Product To Date. Image via SwissBorg</figcaption></figure><p>Thematic investing is a strategy that entails putting your money to work on ideas, personal values, or trends. This holds especially true for new or potentially transformative technology such as blockchain. For reference, the <a href=""https://www.fortunebusinessinsights.com/industry-reports/blockchain-market-100072"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">global blockchain technology market</a> stood at $11.14 billion in 2022 and should reach $17.57 billion in 2023 and $469.49 billion by 2030.&nbsp;</p><p>Thematic investing differs wildly from sector investing.</p><figure class=""table""><table><thead><tr><th>Feature</th><th>Thematic investing</th><th>Sector investing</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Focus</td><td>Multiple sectors anchored around a theme</td><td>Single sector</td></tr><tr><td>Diversification</td><td>Very high</td><td>Minimal</td></tr><tr><td>Investment strategy</td><td>Identifying broader trends expected to shape the future</td><td>Fundamental analysis, growth prospects, etc.</td></tr><tr><td>Risk profile</td><td>Less aggressive</td><td>High-risk, high-reward</td></tr></tbody></table></figure><p>SwissBorg is touting Thematics as its “most advanced” investment product to date. A Thematic is a bundle of crypto assets, grouped around a specific topic. This lowers the barrier to entry as you do not need knowledge of individual tokens.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Thematics_data_e8386387d9.jpg"" alt=""Thematics data.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Thematics_data_e8386387d9.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Thematics_data_e8386387d9.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Thematics_data_e8386387d9.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>SwissBorg Thematics May Be a New Product But It's Already Gaining Traction. Image via SwissBorg</figcaption></figure><h3>Features and Functions</h3><p>Thematics allows you to diversify your investments and minimize risk. Don’t have hours upon hours to sink into research? SwissBorg's analysts and Artificial Intelligence engines will do that for you.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Thematics_features_446c096c06.jpg"" alt=""Thematics features.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Thematics_features_446c096c06.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Thematics_features_446c096c06.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Thematics_features_446c096c06.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Thematics_features_446c096c06.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>An Overview of SwissBorg Thematics' Features. Image via SwissBorg</figcaption></figure><p>Here are a few of its features and functions:</p><ul><li><strong>Quick diversification:</strong> Instead of you having to select cryptos to diversify your portfolio, SwissBorg’s analysts will automate this process for you by picking the best crypto assets, taking into account various factors such as common theme, token performance and tokenomics, among other relevant criteria.</li><li><strong>Quality management: </strong>The SwissBorg team ensures quality management of the Thematics content. This is achieved by keeping the ratio of each token as close to the target as possible, while conducting extensive research to keep Thematics up-to-date, despite market conditions and other risks.</li><li><strong>Rebalancing:</strong> Each thematic crypto asset has an algorithmically optimized target percentage to minimize risks and maximize value. Rebalancing typically occurs every 30 days and depends on when you bought your first Thematic, regardless of any top-ups.</li><li><strong>Reallocation:</strong> SwissBorg always keeps an eye out for new market opportunities and low-performing crypto assets. The tokens and their allocation are changed every 70 days to ensure the Thematic stays true to its theme and performs at its desired level.</li></ul><p>In addition to these, SwissBorg is also looking to roll out a new feature later that will let you earn rewards based on your Thematic balance. These rewards will be paid out on a weekly basis in CHSB, its native token.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/How_to_buy_Thematic_image_f8fb538d3a.jpg"" alt=""How to buy Thematic image.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_How_to_buy_Thematic_image_f8fb538d3a.jpg 193w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_How_to_buy_Thematic_image_f8fb538d3a.jpg 500w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Buying a Thematic That Appeals to You Is Just a Few Clicks Away. Toggle the box to the right to accept, and tap “Next”</li><li>Type the amount that you wish to invest, or select the percentage of your available balance</li><li>Check the Market conditions and then tap “Confirm”</li><li>Tap on Finish and you’re all good.</li></ul><h3>Performance and Fees</h3><p>When it comes to Thematics' performance, SwissBorg hasn't published performance records since March 2023, but users of the SwissBorg app can go in at any time and see how these Thematics have performed, whether they are invested or not. One thing we appreciate about SwissBorg is their dedication to transparency.</p><p>Its last performance update for the Web3 Thematic was in March 2023, and the company hasn't provided performance data for the newer Golden Thematics.&nbsp;</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Web3_Thematic_performance_c472d7b996.jpg"" alt=""Web3 Thematic performance.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Web3_Thematic_performance_c472d7b996.jpg 152w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Web3_Thematic_performance_c472d7b996.jpg 488w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Web3_Thematic_performance_c472d7b996.jpg 731w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Web3 Thematic Was in the Red in March 2023. Overall, the Web3 Thematic was down 5.3%. CHSB, SwissBorg's native token, was among the worst performers.&nbsp;</p><p>Turning to fees, SwissBorg recently lowered the fees it charges for Thematics. Before we dive into that, however, let's first explore the company's plans because the fees depend on what tier you're on.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Swiss_Borg_Plans_63422b86d4.jpg"" alt=""SwissBorg Plans.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Swiss_Borg_Plans_63422b86d4.jpg 241w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Swiss_Borg_Plans_63422b86d4.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Swiss_Borg_Plans_63422b86d4.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>The More CHSB Tokens You're Willing to Lock Away, the More You Can Get Out of SwissBorg. Image via SwissBorg</figcaption></figure><p>Your tier is defined by the number of CSHB tokens you're willing to lock up for a year. Of course, the more you do, the more you can get out of the SwissBorg platform. That means a higher earn boost, and lower exchange and auto-invest fees.</p><p>This mantra also extends to Thematics. Standard, Explorer, Community and Pioneer are charged a monthly subscription of 0.25%, while Generation and Genesis members pay 0.20% per month.&nbsp;</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Swiss_Borg_Thematics_fees_078848a42b.jpg"" alt=""SwissBorg Thematics fees.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_fees_078848a42b.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_fees_078848a42b.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Swiss_Borg_Thematics_fees_078848a42b.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>The New and Improved SwissBorg Thematics Fee Structure. Image via SwissBorg</figcaption></figure><h2>Thematics Products Available</h2><p>SwissBorg currently offers two Thematics products: Web3 and Golden.</p><h3>Web3 Thematic</h3><p>The <a href=""https://www.cognitivemarketresearch.com/web-3.0-market-report"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">global Web3 market</a> size stood at $3.34 billion in 2022 but that number is expected to reach $49.10 billion by 2030. Web3 is the next iteration of the internet, one that’s open, independent and accessible. SwissBorg is betting that as Web3 picks up, so will crypto adoption as it’ll become the currency of the new web.</p><p>Here is a look at the basket of tokens that makes up the Web3 Thematic:</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Web3_Thematic_portfolio_ad7d91fbde.jpg"" alt=""Web3 Thematic portfolio.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Web3_Thematic_portfolio_ad7d91fbde.jpg 172w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Web3_Thematic_portfolio_ad7d91fbde.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Web3_Thematic_portfolio_ad7d91fbde.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Web3 Thematic Gives You Exposure to Many Cryptocurrencies. Image via SwissBorg</figcaption></figure><p>The Web3 Thematic is spread among 13 tokens. <a href=""/review/cosmos-atom/"">Cosmos</a> (ATOM), <a href=""/education/what-is-ethereum/"">Ethereum</a> (ETH), <a href=""/review/polkadot-dot/"">Polkadot</a> (DOT), <a href=""/education/polygon-2023-beginners-guide-to-matic/"">Polygon</a> (MATIC), <a href=""/review/secret-network-scrt/"">Secret</a> (SCRT) and SwissBorg's native CHSB token each have a 10% target ratio. Interestingly, <a href=""/education/what-is-bitcoin/"">Bitcoin</a> isn’t included in the list.</p><h3>Golden Thematic</h3><p>The Golden Thematic capitalizes on Bitcoin's growth potential during market upswings and switches to <a href=""/analysis/bitcoin-vs-gold-inflation-hedge/"">gold</a> during a bear run or downside volatility in a fully automated manner.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Golden_Thematic_95b8bf2d05.jpg"" alt=""Golden Thematic.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Golden_Thematic_95b8bf2d05.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Golden_Thematic_95b8bf2d05.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Golden_Thematic_95b8bf2d05.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Golden Thematics Gives You Exposure to Bitcoin and Gold. Image via SwissBorg</figcaption></figure><p>The Golden Thematic provides access to Gold through Tether Gold (XAUT), a digital token backed by physical gold. Each XAUT token represents 1 troy ounce of gold held in a physical vault. As of March 30, Tether's <a href=""https://assets.ctfassets.net/vyse88cgwfbl/24G4DuQ0HE7h7EQE6vGy4J/8a8a170edf687ea07b3f86048af8b87b/ESO.03.01_Std_ISAE_3000R_Opinion_31-03-2023_BDO_Tether_CRR.pdf"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">gold reserves</a> totalled $3.4 billion. By comparison, XAUT's market cap is $470.2 million, according to <a href=""https://www.coingecko.com/en/coins/tether-gold"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">CoinGecko</a>.&nbsp;</p><p>During different market regimes such as bull, correcting, bear, or accumulating markets, the SwissBorg algorithm adjusts the investment allocations to optimize returns. The reallocations are subject to predefined limits. Unlike the Web3 Thematic, which follows a recurrent schedule and a monthly rebalancing, the Golden Thematic does not have a recurring queue. Instead, you are placed in a random queue upon a new signal, and the SissBorg Smart Engine executes reallocations.</p><p>This is an interesting investing concept as the Golden Thematic looks to capitalize on Bitcoin's upward price movements when they happen and then retreats to the safety of gold to protect against drops in Bitcoin's price.</p><h3>Future Thematics</h3><p>In a YouTube video, SwissBorg laid out options for other such investment products. Before we dive into that, however, I'd like to direct your attention to SwissBorg's native CHSB token.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/CHSB_breakdown_bcab227537.jpg"" alt=""CHSB breakdown.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_CHSB_breakdown_bcab227537.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_CHSB_breakdown_bcab227537.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_CHSB_breakdown_bcab227537.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_CHSB_breakdown_bcab227537.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>The CHSB Utility Token Underpins the SwissBorg Ecosystem. Image via SwissBorg</figcaption></figure><p>The CHSB token is an ERC-20 multi-utility token that embodies the basis of the SwissBorg ecosystem. It can be used for staking and allows you to select and rate ICO projects. More importantly, the token also gives you the power to steer SwissBorg's strategic direction. CHSB can be used by community members to participate in the referendums.</p><p>Right, back to future SwissBorg Thematics.</p><h3><strong>Gaming Thematic</strong></h3><p>In the diverse DApps landscape, gaming reigns supreme. The hallmarks of the best crypto wallets include:</p><ul><li><strong>Private keys:</strong> Wallets that put you in the driver's seat. On the flip side, you're responsible for any loss of funds or mismanagement of keys that may incur.</li><li><strong>Ease of use:</strong> A user interface that's easy on the eyes and a breeze to navigate.</li><li><strong>Development community:</strong> An active development community means better support, frequent updates, and the quick patching of any security vulnerabilities.</li><li><strong>Backup and recovery:</strong> Being able to set up backup and restore features. This typically involves writing down a seed phrase and keeping it somewhere secure.</li><li><strong>Reputation:</strong> A wallet's reputation is an important thing to consider. You can read reviews online to get a sense of the wallet's track record.</li></ul><p>With Ethereum wallets, however, you'll need something that does more.</p><ul><li>Wallets that provide a gateway to interact with decentralized applications (DApps) and decentralized exchanges (DExes)</li><li>The ability to <a href=""/guides/how-to-stake-ethereum/"">stake your ETH</a></li><li><a href=""/adoption/how-safe-is-decentralized-finance/"">DeFi</a> capabilities</li><li>NFT support</li></ul><p>For more on protecting your digital tokens, check out our <a href=""/education/crypto-safety-protect-crypto/"">crypto safety guide</a>.</p><h2>Top 10 Ethereum Wallets</h2><p>The type of wallet you choose determines its specific features and the level of security it provides. The hardware wallet can also be used as a U2F authentication token. In addition, BC VAULT gives you the possibility to store up to 2,000 different anonymous Vaults, each encrypted with a different passcode and pin, making this the only device on the market that can be shared between different users.</p><p>Find out why we called BC Vault “a revolution in cold storage” in our <a href=""/review/bc-vault-review/"">BC Vault review</a>.</p><h3>Rabby</h3><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Rabby_homepage_f5483d6443.jpg"" alt=""Rabby homepage.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Rabby_homepage_f5483d6443.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Rabby_homepage_f5483d6443.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Rabby_homepage_f5483d6443.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Rabby_homepage_f5483d6443.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Rabby's Software is Open Source That Has been Audited. Image via <a href=""https://rabby.io/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Rabby</a></figcaption></figure><figure class=""table""><table><tbody><tr><th>Type of wallet</th><td>Self-custodial software wallet</td></tr><tr><th>Cost</th><td>Free</td></tr><tr><th>Supported crypto</th><td>Ethereum and all ERC-20 tokens</td></tr><tr><th>Available on</th><td>Chrome browser extension and desktop</td></tr><tr><th>Web3 support</th><td>DApps</td></tr><tr><th>Ethereum staking</th><td>No staking support</td></tr></tbody></table></figure><p><a href=""https://rabby.io/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Rabby</a> is designed for multi-chain scenarios and it associates corresponding chain settings for each DeFi DApp. When you visit a DeFi DApp for the first time, Rabby will automatically choose the corresponding chain for this site based on our database.</p><p>Turning to security, Rabby's software is open source and has already been audited by a professional security audit company. In addition, it sends every transaction into a security engine for screening before you sign it to help you identify any hidden risks. Rabby will alert you if it finds potential vulnerabilities. Your private keys are stored on the front-end side only and can be exported by you at any time, which is entirely independent of Rabby’s back-end services.</p><p>Rabby also supports multiple signing methods:</p><ul><li><strong>Hardware wallets</strong>: Ledger, Trezor, GridPlus, OneKey, Keystone, BitBox02, CoolWallet, and AirGap Vault</li><li><strong>Mobile wallets</strong>: MetaMask Mobile, Trust Wallet, imToken, TokenPocket, Math Wallet, Defiant, and all other wallets compatible with WalletConnect</li><li><strong>Institutional wallets</strong>: Gnosis Safe, FireBlocks, Amber, Cobo Wallet, and Jade Wallet</li></ul><p>Rabby wallet is often considered an alternative to MetaMask that focuses on security and transaction verification to help keep the user protected against interaction with malicious smart contracts.</p><h3>MyEtherWallet</h3><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/MEW_homepage_467b98866c.jpg"" alt=""MEW homepage.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_MEW_homepage_467b98866c.jpg 228w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_MEW_homepage_467b98866c.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_MEW_homepage_467b98866c.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_MEW_homepage_467b98866c.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>MEW is the OG Ethereum Wallet. Image via <a href=""https://www.myetherwallet.com/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">MyEtherWallet</a></figcaption></figure><figure class=""table""><table><tbody><tr><th>Type of wallet</th><td>Self-custodial software wallet</td></tr><tr><th>Cost</th><td>Free</td></tr><tr><th>Supported crypto</th><td>Ethereum and all ERC-20 tokens</td></tr><tr><th>Available on</th><td>Chrome browser, mobile app</td></tr><tr><th>Web3 support</th><td>DApps and NFTs</td></tr><tr><th>Ethereum staking</th><td>Yes</td></tr></tbody></table></figure><p><a href=""https://www.myetherwallet.com/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">MyEtherWallet</a> is an open-source wallet that allows you to harness the full power of the Ethereum ecosystem.</p><ul><li><strong>Send ERC-20 tokens and NFTs</strong>: You can send funds to anyone, and view and manage all of your collectables and domains in MEW’s NFT manager.</li><li><strong>Works with other chains</strong>: MEW supports additional Ethereum-compatible networks including Ethereum Classic, Binance Smart Chain and Polygon.</li><li><strong>Swap:</strong> MEW has partnered with 1inch, DEX AG, Changelly, Bity, and Simplex for crypto purchases and swaps. It works with decentralized exchange aggregators 1inch and DEX.AG to find the best price on your token swap.</li><li><strong>DApps centre:</strong> MEW has partnerships with Aave, MakerDAO ENS and Unstoppable Domains. The company said it is constantly on the lookout for more DApps to partner with.</li></ul><p>In addition, you can interact with any smart contract on Ethereum. MEW also has affiliate relationships with a number of hardware wallets including Ledger and Trezor, among others. &nbsp;</p><h3>Phantom Wallet</h3><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Phantom_Wallet_homepage_a003fa9aa3.jpg"" alt=""Phantom Wallet homepage.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Phantom_Wallet_homepage_a003fa9aa3.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Phantom_Wallet_homepage_a003fa9aa3.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Phantom_Wallet_homepage_a003fa9aa3.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>You Can Connect Your Ledger Nano Hardware Wallet with Phantom. Image via <a href=""https://phantom.app/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Phantom Wallet</a></figcaption></figure><figure class=""table""><table><tbody><tr><th>Type of wallet</th><td>Self-custodial mobile and browser extension software wallet</td></tr><tr><th>Cost</th><td>Free</td></tr><tr><th>Supported crypto</th><td>Native support for ETH, SOL and MATIC</td></tr><tr><th>Available on</th><td>Chrome, Brave, Firefox and Edge browsers, as well as iOS and Android</td></tr><tr><th>Web3 support</th><td>DApps and NFTs</td></tr><tr><th>Ethereum staking</th><td>No</td></tr></tbody></table></figure><p>Phantom may have started as a <a href=""/review/solana-sol/"">Solana</a> wallet, but it has since branched out to add support for Ethereum and <a href=""/education/polygon-2023-beginners-guide-to-matic/"">Polygon </a>networks as well. With Phantom, you can:</p><ul><li>Manage your crypto and NFTs</li><li>Stake Solana</li><li>Swap tokens</li><li>Access DeFi applications</li></ul><p>With integrated MoonPay and Coinbase Pay, users can purchase or transfer <a href=""/education/ethereum-2-guide/"">ETH</a>, <a href=""/review/matic-network/"">MATIC</a> and SOL directly from their wallet. You can also connect your Ledger Nano hardware wallet with Phantom. However, this feature is only available on Chrome, Brave and Microsoft Edge web browsers.</p><p>Our full <a href=""/review/phantom-wallet-review/"">Phantom Wallet review</a> covers this and much more!</p><h2>Best Wallets for Ethereum NFTs</h2><p>When it comes to NFTs, Ethereum is the uncontested king. According to <a href=""https://www.coingecko.com/research/publications/market-share-nft-blockchains"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">CoinGecko</a>, the blockchain had a market share of 84.0% and a trading volume of $840 million in June 2023. This underscores the importance of having a dedicated wallet for Ethereum NFTs.</p><p>Here are our top 5 Ethereum wallets for NFTs!</p><ul><li><strong>MetaMask:</strong> It's impossible to talk about crypto wallets and not include MetaMask in the discussion. The MetaMask wallet helps you easily manage, store and transfer your NFTs. For budding blockchain developers out there, the wallet is easy to interact with when building smart contracts for NFTs.</li><li><strong>Trust Wallet:</strong> Trust Wallet provides an easy way to store and access all your crypto collectables. It boasts a user-friendly mobile app, you can buy and sell NFTs directly on several marketplaces, and you can easily access DApps to stake your NFTs.</li><li><strong>Ledger:</strong> This is a hardware wallet that lets you automatically display your Ethereum blockchain-based NFTs on the Ledger Live mobile app. The company's NFT partners include Rainbow me and Poap, with Rarible coming soon.</li><li><a href=""/review/zengo/""><strong>Zengo</strong></a><strong>:</strong> A self-custodial crypto wallet with no seed phrase vulnerability, Zengo has over 9000,000 users. Zengo’s NFT wallet app lets you view your NFT collection without leaving the app, and it supports both Ethereum and Polygon. Using WalletConnnect, you can purchase, sell and trade NFTs.</li><li><a href=""https://enjin.io/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener""><strong>Enjin</strong></a><strong>:</strong> This mobile wallet provides an end-to-end solution needed to launch NFT projects. It lets you create, distribute, and integrate NFTs via a simple interface. It has been installed by over 2.3 million users.</li></ul><h2>Best Ethereum Wallets for DeFi</h2><p>Ethereum's DApps landscape is diverse, running the gamut from decentralized exchanges to gaming platforms. But the top-10 DApps on Ethereum are mostly DeFi, which serves as an alternative to the current financial system.</p><p>If you're in the market for a long-term solution, Trezor, BC Vault, Ledger and ELLIPAL would be good choices as they're hardware wallets, resulting in a <a href=""/education/crypto-safety-protect-crypto/"">higher level of security than software wallets</a>. These wallets securely keep your private keys in cold storage, meaning they are not connected to the internet. So, if you aren't looking to cash out on that crypto nest egg anytime soon, this would be the way to go.</p><p>With regards to DeFi specifically, MetaMask is an accessible entry point to connect to the world of DeFi. It lets you swap crypto, utilizing data from decentralized exchanges and market makers to ensure you get the best prices. Looking to earn yield on your crypto? MetaMask lets you stake ETH and MATIC.</p><p>If convenience is your thing, Wallet Connect's integration with Trust Wallet and other wallets brings a host of quality-of-life improvements for DeFi. You can subscribe to push notifications directly from your favourite DApps.</p><p><a href=""https://guy.coinbureau.com/signup/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Newsletter_inline_a4c7553089.jpg"" alt=""Newsletter Inline"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Newsletter_inline_a4c7553089.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Newsletter_inline_a4c7553089.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Newsletter_inline_a4c7553089.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""></a></p><h2>Ethereum Staking Support</h2><p>There aren't a whole lot of wallets offering Ethereum staking support. That said, MyEtherWallet opened support for ETH staking, offering:</p><ul><li>Full validator staking of 32 ETH is supported via Staked.us</li><li>Liquid staking through StakeWise and Lido</li></ul><p>In addition, Exodus also allows you to connect to Lido with Exodus Web3 wallet or its mobile app to stake ETH. Another wallet offering Ethereum staking support is MetaMask, which lets you stake ETH via Lido and Rocket Pool.</p><h2>Best Ethereum Wallets: Closing Thoughts</h2><p>Choosing the right Ethereum wallet can make a difference in the limitations and functionalities available to the user. The best wallets combine security, ease of use, developer support, and a good reputation to offer a well-rounded product. However, with regards to Ethereum specifically, you may wanna be on the lookout for wallets that also provide additional features like DApp and DeFi capabilities, NFT support, and even Ethereum staking.</p>"https://www.coinbureau.com/Analysis/best-tron-dapps/,8 Best Tron DApps 2023: Top Projects on TRX!,Analysis,https://www.coinbureau.com/Analysis/evolution-of-bitcoin/,How Bitcoin has Evolved from Satoshi's Original Vision,Analysis,https://www.coinbureau.com/Analysis/ethereum-dominance/,Ethereum Dominance: ETH vs. Other Blockchains,Analysis,https://www.coinbureau.com/Analysis/best-ethereum-dapps/,Ethereum Dapps: 10 Decentralized Apps You Can Use Right Now,Analysis,"<!-- wp:paragraph --><p>The <a href=""/education/what-is-ethereum/"">Ethereum Network</a> is at the forefront of innovation in the crypto market and it's all thanks to the pioneering <a href=""/education/ethereum-smart-contracts/"">smart contracts</a>.</p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p>At the heart of this platform lies an ecosystem of decentralized applications, or DApps, which have changed the way we interact with digital systems. These apps range from gaming and gambling to asset exchanges and finance to media and social DApps and more.</p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p>Whether you're a curious explorer or a crypto degen, join us as we explore the 10 best Ethereum DApps.</p><figure class=""image""><a href=""/deals/trading/okx/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/OKX_Inline_4c6ce0ceba.jpg"" alt=""OKX Inline"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_OKX_Inline_4c6ce0ceba.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_OKX_Inline_4c6ce0ceba.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_OKX_Inline_4c6ce0ceba.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""></a></figure><h2>What are Ethereum DApps?</h2><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:heading --><p>While the blockchain is an immutable ledger, Ethereum has taken the <a href=""/education/what-is-blockchain-technology/"">blockchain</a> further through the creation of smart contracts that allow developers to create open-source software built on the back of the blockchain to leverage its many advantages.</p><!-- wp:html --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p>Because the blockchain is decentralized, the applications built on top of a blockchain are also decentralized, meaning they have no central authority or ownership. Once a DApp is deployed even the developers no longer have control over it.</p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p>Common features of an Ethereum DApp are:</p><!-- wp:list --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><ul><li><strong>Open Source:</strong> DApps should ideally be open-source software with the code able to be examined and proven free of malicious code.</li><li><strong>Decentralized: </strong>Ethereum DApps are built on a decentralized blockchain, and any changes should be determined by the consensus of user votes.</li><li><strong>Incentivized:</strong> Users who act as validators of transactions on the blockchain should be provided incentives in the form of digital tokens for their activity.</li><li><strong>Protocol:</strong> The community of application developers and users must agree on the cryptographic algorithm used to show proof of value. In the case of Ethereum, this is currently Proof-of-Stake (PoS).</li></ul><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/ETH_TVL_eb62bbb699.jpg"" alt=""Ethereum Dapps"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_ETH_TVL_eb62bbb699.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_ETH_TVL_eb62bbb699.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_ETH_TVL_eb62bbb699.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Ethereum's TVL Blows Past the Competition. Image via <a href=""https://dappradar.com/blog/state-of-the-dapp-industry-in-q2-2023"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DappRadar</a></figcaption></figure><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:list --><p>In the second quarter of 2023, Ethereum's total value locked (TVL) was higher than its competitors by a wide margin. Based on data collected by DappRadar, there are well over 4,000 Ethereum DApps.</p><!-- wp:heading --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><h2>Types of Ethereum DApps</h2><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:heading --><p>While the categorization of DApps is broader, the Ethereum white paper has identified and defined three types of DApps:</p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p><strong>DApps to Manage Money</strong></p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p>This is the most common type of DApp and consists of an application that requires one user to pay Ether to settle a smart contract and receive some good, service or data.</p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p><strong>DApps to Manage Money Involving Outside Information</strong></p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p>This type of DApp requires payment in Ether, and also requires the input of some outside information. One good example of this is Augur and other prediction market DApps. In any prediction market, there will be an outside event and the outcome of that event is required to settle the contract.</p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p><strong>DApps Managing Voting and Governance</strong></p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p>When managing governance or voting most DApps make use of Decentralized Autonomous Organizations (DAOs). By doing so they can create truly decentralized apps with no reliance on a centralized board of leadership hierarchy. Rules regarding voting and consensus as well as the distribution of funds are all set when the DAO is initialized, and the dApps can then continue to run forever.</p><!-- wp:heading --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><h2>Top 10 Ethereum DApps</h2><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:heading --><p>The top-10 DApps on Ethereum are in the decentralized finance space.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/ETH_top_D_Apps_30e22ac1d7.jpg"" alt=""Best Ethereum Dapps.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_ETH_top_D_Apps_30e22ac1d7.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_ETH_top_D_Apps_30e22ac1d7.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_ETH_top_D_Apps_30e22ac1d7.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_ETH_top_D_Apps_30e22ac1d7.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Most of the Top-10 DApps are in the DeFi Space. Image via <a href=""https://defillama.com/chain/Ethereum"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DefiLlama</a></figcaption></figure><p>However, for the sake of diversity, we're going to list DApps across different categories, but you're going to see some names from this list as well.</p><h3>1. Uniswap</h3><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:heading --><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Uniswap_TVL_55bff1c091.jpg"" alt=""Uniswap TVL.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Uniswap_TVL_55bff1c091.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Uniswap_TVL_55bff1c091.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Uniswap_TVL_55bff1c091.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Uniswap_TVL_55bff1c091.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Uniswap's TVL Stood at $3.3 billion on Sept. 7. Image via <a href=""https://defillama.com/protocol/uniswap"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DefiLlama</a></figcaption></figure><p><a href="""" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Uniswap</a> is an open-source protocol for providing liquidity and trading ERC-20 tokens on Ethereum. It is an automated market maker. In practical terms, it is a collection of smart contracts that define a standard way to create liquidity pools, provide liquidity, and swap assets. Uniswap has thus far seen $1.5 trillion worth of trading volume and trades of over 156 million.</p><p>There is a 0.3% fee for swapping tokens. This fee is split by liquidity providers proportional to their contribution to liquidity reserves. Uniswap currently doesn't charge protocol fees. However, it is possible for a 0.05% fee to be turned on in the future.</p><h3>2. Lido</h3><p><a href=""https://lido.fi/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Lido</a> is a decentralized liquid staking protocol with a total value locked of $14.2 billion, virtually all of which it generates through Ethereum.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Lido_TVL_caa0302289.jpg"" alt=""Lido TVL.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Lido_TVL_caa0302289.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Lido_TVL_caa0302289.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Lido_TVL_caa0302289.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Lido_TVL_caa0302289.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Lido is Currently the Largest DApp on Ethereum. Image via <a href=""https://defillama.com/protocol/lido"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DefiLlama</a></figcaption></figure><p>According to <a href=""https://twitter.com/DefiLlama/status/1651309741132447745?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw%7Ctwcamp%5Etweetembed%7Ctwterm%5E1651309741132447745%7Ctwgr%5E2b50a9376bed1cfe5e705484e92eef56b27d6ba7%7Ctwcon%5Es1_&amp;ref_url=https%3A%2F%2Fcointelegraph.com%2Fnews%2Fliquid-staking-solutions-now-have-more-tvl-than-dexs-defi-llama"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DefiLlama</a>, liquid staking protocols have surpassed decentralized exchanges in total value locked, making it the leading category in DeFi by TVL dominance.</p><p>Lido boasts close to 300,000 stakers, and it has paid out over $680 million in total rewards. The staking protocol applies a 10% fee on staking rewards that are split between node operators, and the DAO Treasury.&nbsp;</p><p>It offers an APR of 3.6% on Ethereum, 4.2% on Polygon and 6.7% on Solana. &nbsp;</p><h3>3. Decentraland</h3><p><a href=""https://{MIGRATED_DOMAIN}/review/decentraland-mana/"">Decentraland</a> is an open-source virtual social world powered by the Ethereum blockchain. In its metaverse, you can personalize your character, create virtual buildings, and monetize from doing so.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Dentraland_plot_for_sale_4f2510ecce.jpg"" alt=""Dentraland plot for sale.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Dentraland_plot_for_sale_4f2510ecce.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Dentraland_plot_for_sale_4f2510ecce.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Dentraland_plot_for_sale_4f2510ecce.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Dentraland_plot_for_sale_4f2510ecce.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>A 3x3 Plot is For Sale on Decentraland for Over $205,000. Image via <a href=""https://market.decentraland.org/contracts/0x959e104e1a4db6317fa58f8295f586e1a978c297/tokens/5025"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Decentraland</a></figcaption></figure><p>Lands are the most important in the Decentraland virtual world. The company has incubated a variety of entertainment events, including Fashion Week and Metaverse Music Festival. Brands including Samsung, Nike, Cola-Cola and Adidas have hosted experiences in the venue as well.</p><p>What would a virtual world be without experiencing it in virtual reality? Decentraland is also available for the Meta Quest. According to <a href=""https://dappradar.com/dapp/decentraland?range-ds=30d&amp;range-ha=30d"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DappRadar</a>, the company has seen volume of more than $590,000 over the past 30 days.</p><h3>4. MakerDao</h3><p>Use crypto to borrow crypto!</p><p><a href=""https://makerdao.com/en/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">MakerDao</a> is a decentralized company built on Ethereum. It has created a protocol allowing anyone with ETH to lend themselves money in the form of a stablecoin called DAI.&nbsp;</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Marker_DAO_TVL_430cc3f42a.jpg"" alt=""MarkerDAO TVL.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Marker_DAO_TVL_430cc3f42a.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Marker_DAO_TVL_430cc3f42a.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Marker_DAO_TVL_430cc3f42a.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Marker_DAO_TVL_430cc3f42a.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>MakerDAO Drives All of its TVL from Ethereum. Image via <a href=""https://defillama.com/protocol/makerdao"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DefiLlama</a></figcaption></figure><p>Here's how it works: By locking up some ETH in MakerDAO's smart contracts (known as collateralized debt positions) as collateral, you can create a DAI, its native digital token. The more ETH you lock up, the more DAI you can create. When users are ready to unlock their ETH, they simply pay back the loan along with any fees.</p><p>Speaking of fees, you can expect to pay a “<a href=""https://twitter.com/MakerDaiBot/status/1658924924201848835"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">stability fee</a>” of between 0.5% and 1.75%. The company explains that this fee is a risk parameter designed to address imbalances in supply and demand for the Dai token which could result from periods of low or negative growth in the cryptocurrency markets.</p><h3>5. Aave</h3><p>The third-largest Ethereum DApp by TVL is <a href=""https://aave.com/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Aave</a>, an open-source, non-custodial protocol to earn interest on deposits and borrow assets.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/AAVE_TVL_85457d5060.jpg"" alt=""AAVE TVL.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_AAVE_TVL_85457d5060.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_AAVE_TVL_85457d5060.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_AAVE_TVL_85457d5060.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_AAVE_TVL_85457d5060.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Aave is the Third-Largest Ethereum DApp. Image via <a href=""https://defillama.com/protocol/aave"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DefiLlama</a></figcaption></figure><p>Of its $4.55 billion TVL, Aave drives the bulk of it through Ethereum, and the rest through Polygon and Avalanche, among others. To date, about $10 billion of liquidity is locked in Aave across five networks and over 11 markets.</p><p>The protocol has a strong emphasis on security. It receives blockchain intelligence from TRM Labs, which combines on-chain data and real-world investigations to identify financial crime and other prohibited activities.</p><h3>6. dYdX</h3><p><a href=""https://dydx.exchange/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">dYdX</a> trading platform for crypto assets that recently moved to Layer 2 amid scaling issues in Layer 1.&nbsp;</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/dydx_TVL_58393ad3c0.jpg"" alt=""dydx TVL.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_dydx_TVL_58393ad3c0.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_dydx_TVL_58393ad3c0.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_dydx_TVL_58393ad3c0.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_dydx_TVL_58393ad3c0.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>dYdX's TVL Stood at $338.8 Million as of Sept. 7. Image via <a href=""https://defillama.com/protocol/dydx"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DefiLlama</a></figcaption></figure><p>The move to Layer 2 will result in low fees and no gas fee, fast withdrawals, and instant execution of trades, the company said. The dYdX platform is used by over 250,000 traders, and the company witnessed more than $535 million in trading over the past 24 hours.</p><p>There are no fees associated with deposits or withdrawals on dYdX. The maker fee ranges from -0.0085% ($200 million-plus volume ) to 0.020%, and the taker fee is between 0.020% and 0.050%.</p><h3>7. Nexus Mutual</h3><p><a href=""https://nexusmutual.io/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Nexus Mutual</a> offers decentralized insurance against smart contract failure. It currently offers two products.</p><ul><li><strong>Protocol cover: </strong>This allows you to cover assets deposited in a single protocol against a range of loss events, including hacks, exploits, oracle failure, liquidation failure and governance attacks.</li><li><strong>ETH Slashing cover:</strong> This secures against losses incurred from penalties in the Ethereum consensus process.</li></ul><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Nexus_Mutual_TVL_7f9399be94.jpg"" alt=""Nexus Mutual TVL.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Nexus_Mutual_TVL_7f9399be94.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Nexus_Mutual_TVL_7f9399be94.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Nexus_Mutual_TVL_7f9399be94.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Nexus_Mutual_TVL_7f9399be94.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Nexus Mutual's TVL Was $228.4 Million as of Sept. 7. Image via <a href=""https://defillama.com/protocol/nexus-mutual"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DefiLlama</a> &nbsp;</figcaption></figure><p>The Nexus Mutual protocol is built on Ethereum and provides the infrastructure for members to buy cover, underwrite risk, assess claims, and build risk management businesses.</p><p>The company plans to launch a directors-and-officers cover as well as protection against real-world risks soon.</p><h3>8. Yearn Finance</h3><p><a href=""https://yearn.fi/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Yearn Finance</a> is an aggregator service for DeFi investors. It uses automation to allow them to maximize profits from yield farming.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Yearn_Finance_TVL_c3fddc22be.jpg"" alt=""Yearn Finance TVL.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Yearn_Finance_TVL_c3fddc22be.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Yearn_Finance_TVL_c3fddc22be.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Yearn_Finance_TVL_c3fddc22be.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Yearn_Finance_TVL_c3fddc22be.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Yearn Finance Had TVL of over $360 million as of Sept. 7. Image via <a href=""https://defillama.com/protocol/yearn-finance"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">DefiLlama</a>&nbsp;</figcaption></figure><p>Yearn Finance's Vaults act as capital pools that automatically generate yield based on opportunities present in the market. Vaults benefit users by socializing gas costs, automating the yield generation and rebalancing process, and automatically shifting capital as opportunities arise.</p><h3>9. Illuvium</h3><p><a href=""https://illuvium.io/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Illuvium</a> has an ambitious vision: To build the first Interoperable blockchain game universe including an open-world exploration game, industrial city builder, and autobattler, all on the Ethereum blockchain.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Illubium_games_abb64a41f4.jpg"" alt=""Illuvium games.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Illubium_games_abb64a41f4.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Illubium_games_abb64a41f4.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Illubium_games_abb64a41f4.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Illubium_games_abb64a41f4.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>A Catalog of Illuvium's Gaming Universe. Image via Illuvium</figcaption></figure><p>Illuvium gives the users complete ownership over their in-game assets, which are all stored on their Ethereum wallet. Each asset is verifiable on the Ethereum blockchain, proving your ownership.</p><!-- wp:heading {""level"":3} --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><h3>10. Storj</h3><p>Solve cloud storage problems with blockchain technology!</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Storj_homepage_e29d826c5c.jpg"" alt=""Storj homepage.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Storj_homepage_e29d826c5c.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Storj_homepage_e29d826c5c.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Storj_homepage_e29d826c5c.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Storj_homepage_e29d826c5c.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Storj Leverages Blockchain Technology to Solve Cloud Storage Problems. Image via Storj</figcaption></figure><p><a href=""https://www.storj.io/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Storj</a> is a crypto-powered cloud storage platform that allows anyone with a little extra space in their hard drive to rent it out to users looking to store files. The data is automatically encrypted and then split into pieces. Next, these pieces are individually distributed to uncorrelated nodes around the world.</p><p>Users pay for storage space with its native token, an ERC-20 token that works on the Ethereum blockchain.</p><p><a href=""https://t.me/cbinsider"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Telegram_inline_fe7d5fe2dc.jpg"" alt=""Telegram Inline"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Telegram_inline_fe7d5fe2dc.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Telegram_inline_fe7d5fe2dc.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Telegram_inline_fe7d5fe2dc.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""></a></p><h2>Conclusion</h2><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:heading --><p>In the past few years, the number of DApps on the Ethereum blockchain has exploded.</p><!-- wp:paragraph --><!-- /wp:paragraph --><p>As the ecosystem grows, and as Ethereum scales, the number of DApps is likely to explode ever more. TOKEN2049 is a global meeting place for entrepreneurs, institutions, industry insiders, investors, builders, and those with a strong interest in the crypto and blockchain industry.</p><p><strong>Media Contact</strong></p><p><a href=""mailto:token2049sg@wachsman.com"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">token2049sg@wachsman.com</a></p>"https://www.coinbureau.com/Analysis/crypto-vs-sp-500-2023/,Crypto vs. S&P 500 Performance in 2023,Analysis,"<p>The investment environment has widened beyond its traditional boundaries since cryptocurrencies arrived on the scene, and threatened the dominance of the S&amp;P 500, which, as the name suggests, represents 500 of the largest publicly traded companies in the U.S.</p><p>Cryptocurrencies, which emerged from the ashes of the 2008 financial crisis, have attracted interest from both risk-tolerant mom-and-pop investors, and mainstream financial institutions, who have had a change of heart since Bitcoin’s nascent days. While crypto represents a departure from conventional financial practices, the S&amp;P 500 provides stability and is a testament to the traditional markets’ lasting strength.</p><p><i><strong>Disclaimer:</strong> I hold BTC and ETH.</i></p><p><a href=""/deals/trading/swissborg/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener""><i><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Swissborg_inline_57564f04fd.jpg"" alt=""Swissborg inline"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Swissborg_inline_57564f04fd.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Swissborg_inline_57564f04fd.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Swissborg_inline_57564f04fd.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""></i></a></p><p>In this Crypto vs. S&amp;P 500 Analysis, we are going to compare, contrast, and explore each market in terms of ROI, but first, a bit of background.&nbsp;</p><h2>What is the S&amp;P 500?</h2><p><a href=""https://www.spglobal.com/spdji/en/indices/equity/sp-500/#overview"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">The S&amp;P 500</a>, one of the most widely followed equity indices, tracks the performance of 500 of the largest companies listed in the U.S. and covers approximately 80% of available market capitalization. An estimated $15.6 trillion is indexed or benchmarked to the index.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/S_and_P_500_sector_breakdown_5e1fdfa87d.jpg"" alt=""S&amp;P 500 sector breakdown"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_S_and_P_500_sector_breakdown_5e1fdfa87d.jpg 173w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_S_and_P_500_sector_breakdown_5e1fdfa87d.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_S_and_P_500_sector_breakdown_5e1fdfa87d.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>The IT Sector Is The Largest Constituent of The S&amp;P 500. Image via <a href=""https://www.spglobal.com/spdji/en/indices/equity/sp-500/#data"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">S&amp;P Global</a></figcaption></figure><p>The IT sector comprises the lion’s share of the index. In fact, the five largest companies — Apple, Microsoft, Amazon.com, Nvidia and Alphabet — are all IT firms. Healthcare makes up 13.1% and financial companies round out the top three with a 12.6% share of the index.</p><p>S&amp;P 500 traces its roots to 1923 when <a href=""https://www.britannica.com/topic/Standard-and-Poors"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Standard and Poor’s</a> introduced an index covering 233 companies weekly. The index, in its current form, was created in 1957 and would go on to become the most widely used proxy of the U.S. stock market. The index is maintained by a group of S&amp;P’s economists and index analysts.</p><h3>Why is the S&amp;P 500 so Important?</h3><p>The S&amp;P 500 is a stalwart index representing the largest publicly traded companies in the U.S. It stands as a cornerstone of the conventional investment market and is renowned for its stability and historical significance.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/S_and_P_500_returns_over_20_years_4c034452f6.jpg"" alt=""S&amp;P 500 returns over 20 years"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_S_and_P_500_returns_over_20_years_4c034452f6.jpg 244w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_S_and_P_500_returns_over_20_years_4c034452f6.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_S_and_P_500_returns_over_20_years_4c034452f6.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>The S&amp;P 500 Has Posted More Gains Than Losses in the Last 20 Years. Image via <a href=""https://www.macrotrends.net/2526/sp-500-historical-annual-returns"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Macro Trends</a></figcaption></figure><p>The S&amp;P 500 holds significant sway in the financial world due to several factors that make it an important benchmark and indicator of the overall health and performance of the U.S. stock market.</p><ul><li><strong>Representative of economic health:</strong> As noted, the S&amp;P 500 comprises some of the largest public companies in the U.S. When read alongside other government data, the index is considered a reliable barometer of how well or bad the economy is performing.&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Investor sentiment:</strong> The S&amp;P 500 is far from the only stock market index in the U.S.; the Dow Jones Industrial Average and the Nasdaq 100 are two other majors. But the S&amp;P 500 is the most widely followed index. As a result, it's performance is used to determine investors’ perception of current and future economic conditions.</li><li><strong>Global impact:</strong> As the U.S. is the largest economy in the world, its markets' influence extends beyond its borders. Indeed, U.S. equity markets <a href=""https://www.sifma.org/resources/research/research-quarterly-equities/#:~:text=The%20U.S.%20equity%20markets%20are,the%20next%20largest%20market%2C%20China."" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">represent</a> 42.5% of the global equity market cap. As a result, the S&amp;P 500's performance on any day impacts global financial markets from Asia to Europe. &nbsp;</li><li><strong>Market cap weighting:</strong> This means that companies with larger market values have a proportionally greater impact on the index's performance. This approach to market capitalization weighting reflects the size and influence of different companies within the economy.</li><li><strong>Historical data:</strong> The index in its current form came into existence more than 65 years ago. It provides a treasure trove of data to help anyone analyze market trends, economic cycles and the effects of market-moving events.</li></ul><h2>S&amp;P 500 Historical Performance</h2><p>Between 1965 and 2022, the S&amp;P 500 returned an average of <a href=""https://www.businessinsider.com/personal-finance/average-stock-market-return#:~:text=There%20are%20many%20stock%20market,return%20in%202022%20was%2018.1%25."" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">9.9%</a>. Its highest return was in 1995, just before the dot-com bubble, when the index returned 34.11%. In 2008, when the housing market crisis was in full swing, the S&amp;P 500 was down 38.49%. For most traditional investors, a 9.9% average return isn’t too shabby at all.</p><p>Overall, the index has returned a profit more times than it has turned red.</p><p>Most crypto investors would scoff at these returns. After all, investors in the crypto sphere can blow past these returns with their eyes closed. <a href=""/review/axie-infinity/"">Axie Infinity</a>, then a small-cap altcoin, rewarded investors with a mind-boggling 71,910.71% return in a single year. But that’s not all! <a href=""/education/what-is-bitcoin/"">Bitcoin</a>, the largest crypto by market cap, returned over 5,000% in 2013, and <a href=""/education/what-is-ethereum/"">Ethereum's</a> return was 10,000% in 2017.</p><p>For traditional stock market investors, these returns are probably both head-scratchers and unattainable.</p><h2>Top 10 Crypto Historical Performance</h2><p>The first Bitcoin was minted in 2009. While crypto may be the new kid on the block, and as such, has a lot to prove to the traditionally minded investor, the past few years have been nothing short of remarkable (with the occasional bumps in the road).</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Bitcoin_vs_gold_0536f8ce7e.jpg"" alt=""Bitcoin vs gold.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Bitcoin_vs_gold_0536f8ce7e.jpg 233w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Bitcoin_vs_gold_0536f8ce7e.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Bitcoin_vs_gold_0536f8ce7e.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Bitcoin_vs_gold_0536f8ce7e.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Gold Has Flatlined over 14 Years While Bitcoin Has Rocketted. Image via <a href=""https://charts.woobull.com/bitcoin-vs-gold/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">charts.woodbull</a></figcaption></figure><p>This chart looks at how much money you’d make if you had invested $1 in Bitcoin and gold 14 years ago. Investing in gold, a traditional safe haven asset class, would make you $1.93 over 14 years. Bitcoin? Over $3.8 million, that’s a fat return on a mere buck! So much for gold being much of an <a href=""/analysis/bitcoin-vs-gold-inflation-hedge/"">inflation hedge.</a></p><p>But enough about Bitcoin.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/S_and_P_500_vs_Crypto_performance_afa8334a14.jpg"" alt=""S&amp;P 500 vs Crypto performance.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_S_and_P_500_vs_Crypto_performance_afa8334a14.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_S_and_P_500_vs_Crypto_performance_afa8334a14.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_S_and_P_500_vs_Crypto_performance_afa8334a14.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_S_and_P_500_vs_Crypto_performance_afa8334a14.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>A Look at the Top Coins By Market Cap. Image via <a href=""https://www.coingecko.com/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">CoinGecko</a></figcaption></figure><p>The top-10 cryptocurrencies often trade places. Some move down the list, while others gain a rank or two. Favorites such as Bitcoin and Ethereum continue to maintain their first and second spot, respectively. But there is a surprise entrant that has managed to break into the coveted top-10 group.</p><p><a href=""/review/dogecoin-friendliest-cryptocurrency/"">Doge</a>, a meme coin started as a joke, sits at No. 9. Tesla founder and billionaire Elon Musk has arguably been Doge’s biggest proponent. <a href=""/news/dogecoin-soaring-after-elon-musk-says-tesla-will-sell-merch-for-doge/"">His tweets</a>, which are often, are a seismic event for the cryptocurrency. Anytime he tweets about Doge, the meme coin’s price tends to surge.</p><p>In addition, two <a href=""/guides/guide-to-stablecoins/"">stablecoins</a> are in there as well — <a href=""/education/what-is-tether-usdt/"">Tether</a> (No. 3) and <a href=""/education/what-is-the-usdc-stablecoin/"">USD Coin</a> (No. 6). Some favorites such as <a href=""/review/litecoin-ltc/"">Litecoin</a>, <a href=""/education/polygon-2023-beginners-guide-to-matic/"">Polygon</a>, <a href=""/review/tron-trx-review/"">TRON</a> and <a href=""/review/polkadot-dot/"">Polkadot</a> have fallen off the top 10 mark.</p><p>To track how our top-10 group has fared, we’ll take help from the <a href=""https://www.six-group.com/en/products-services/financial-information/indices/crypto-indices/crypto-market-index-10.html"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Crypto Market Index 10</a> (CMI10), which tracks the performance of, you guessed it, top-10 cryptocurrencies. As a reminder, S&amp;P 500 investors fetch an average return of just under 10% each year.</p><p>Year to date, the Crypto Market Index 10 is up 47.25%. The S&amp;P 500 is up only 14.44%.</p><h3>Bitcoin</h3><p>First minted in 2009 by the elusive Satoshi Nakamoto (nobody knows their true identity), the granddaddy of all cryptocurrencies has since turned naysayers into believers. <a href=""https://originstamp.com/blog/how-many-banks-are-using-cryptocurrency/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Examples</a> include mega financial institutions like BNY Mellon, Citibank, Morgan Stanley and Goldman Sachs, who all agreed to invest in the space.</p><p>The <a href=""https://www.proshares.com/our-etfs/strategic/bito"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">ProShares Bitcoin Strategy ETF's</a> (BITO) launch in October 2021 kicked off a flurry of other such funds being made available for the public to invest. Global X also introduced three new exchange-traded products in Europe. <a href=""https://grayscale.com/products/grayscale-bitcoin-trust/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">The Grayscale Bitcoin Trust </a>launched to much fanfare as well. It currently boasts over $16 billion in assets under management.</p><p>These <a href=""/analysis/crypto-investment-products/"">investment products</a> are just a few among many Bitcoin ETFs, Bitcoin mutual funds and Bitcoin futures. Of course, you can also trade bitcoin as you would any stock listed on an exchange by using a <a href=""/review/best-crypto-exchanges/"">reputable crypto exchange.</a></p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Bitcoin_vs_stocks_5da1ea59a7.jpg"" alt=""Bitcoin vs stocks"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Bitcoin_vs_stocks_5da1ea59a7.jpg 230w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Bitcoin_vs_stocks_5da1ea59a7.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Bitcoin_vs_stocks_5da1ea59a7.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Bitcoin_vs_stocks_5da1ea59a7.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Bitcoin's Growth Outpaces Stocks. Image via <a href=""https://charts.woobull.com/bitcoin-growth-vs-other-assets/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Woobull</a></figcaption></figure><p>It wouldn’t be wrong to say that Bitcoin has proven its value as an asset class, store of value and a hedge against inflation. Bitcoin’s growth not only outpaces stocks generally, but tech stocks specifically as well. As a reminder, tech companies are the S&amp;P 500’s largest constituent.</p><p>Turning to returns, in no surprise to anyone, Bitcoin outpaces every other major stock market index.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Bitcoin_ROI_vs_other_major_indexes_56ce5a6aaa.jpg"" alt=""Bitcoin ROI vs other major indexes"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Bitcoin_ROI_vs_other_major_indexes_56ce5a6aaa.jpg 138w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Bitcoin_ROI_vs_other_major_indexes_56ce5a6aaa.jpg 441w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Bitcoin_ROI_vs_other_major_indexes_56ce5a6aaa.jpg 661w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Bitcoins ROI Blows Past Every Major Stock Market Index in The U.S. Image via <a href=""https://finbold.com/bitcoin-vs-indexes-q1-2023/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Finbold</a></figcaption></figure><p>S&amp;P 500’s 6.36% return in the first quarter of 2023 and NASDAQ Composite’s decent 17.39% return pale in comparison to Bitcoin’s return on investment of 69.4% during the period. It’s important to note that the quarter saw regulators seizing a number of banks in high-profile closures, which prompted the Average Joe to call into question the health of the entire financial system.</p><h3>Ethereum</h3><p>The second most popular cryptocurrency has earned itself the moniker “digital oil.” This analogy is not an official designation but rather a way to highlight Ethereum's role in powering a wide range of decentralized applications and services through its <a href=""/education/ethereum-smart-contracts/"">smart contract</a> capabilities. Many crypto enthusiasts argue that Bitcoin doesn’t have a real utility other than a store of value. Ethereum, however, is an entirely different story.</p><ul><li><strong>Foundation for DApps:</strong> Ethereum provides a foundational platform for building decentralized applications, which can span across finance, supply chain management, gaming and more.</li><li><strong>Smart contracts:</strong> Ethereum's smart contract functionality enables the creation of self-executing contracts with predefined rules and conditions. This has opened the door to decentralized finance applications, which allow for complex financial interactions without intermediaries.</li><li><strong>Digital transformation:</strong> Just as the discovery and utilization of oil transformed industries and economies, Ethereum has the potential to transform the digital landscape by enabling new business models and interactions through blockchain technology.</li></ul><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Etheruem_returns_490482f4bf.jpg"" alt=""Etheruem returns"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Etheruem_returns_490482f4bf.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Etheruem_returns_490482f4bf.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Etheruem_returns_490482f4bf.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Etheruem Has Been Going Strong Lately. Image via <a href=""https://www.upmyinterest.com/fund?tick=Ethereum"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">UpMyInterest</a></figcaption></figure><p>Ethereum’s mean annual return is 194.4%. In 2022, the cryptocurrency’s return on investment was over 300%.</p><h3>Binance Coin</h3><p><a href=""/review/binance-coin-bnb/"">Binance Coin</a> (BNB) is the native cryptocurrency of <a href=""/review/binance-vs-binance-us-review/"">Binance</a>, the world's largest and most popular cryptocurrency exchange in terms of daily trading volume. Binance Coin was initially launched as an Ethereum-based token but was later migrated to Binance's own blockchain, known as the Binance Smart Chain (now called BNB Chain), where it operates as the native digital asset.</p><p>In 2017, when BNB was launched to the public, the coin’s value was $0.15. It reached an all-time high of $690 in 2021. That is an astronomically staggering 459,900% return.</p><p>Over time, Binance Coin has gained significant popularity and value due to its association and utility with one of the most influential cryptocurrency exchanges and BNB Chain network. It has grown beyond being just a utility token for the Binance platform and has become a tradable asset in its own right, often included in various cryptocurrency portfolios.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/BNB_Performance_0ba5f1660c.jpg"" alt=""BNB Performance.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_BNB_Performance_0ba5f1660c.jpg 201w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_BNB_Performance_0ba5f1660c.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_BNB_Performance_0ba5f1660c.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_BNB_Performance_0ba5f1660c.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Binance Coin's Price Took A Hammering After SEC Sued The Exchange. Thanks for the “Protection,” Gary. Image via CoinGecko</figcaption></figure><p>Binance's native token took a hammering in June after the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission <a href=""https://www.sec.gov/news/press-release/2023-101"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">sued the exchange</a>.</p><p>Year to date, the token is down 11.79%. Over the last year, it has fallen 28.69%. However, since inception, the token is still up a mind-boggling 187,158.36%</p><h3>XRP</h3><p>Fresh off a <a href=""https://www.reuters.com/legal/us-judge-says-sec-lawsuit-vs-ripple-labs-can-proceed-trial-some-claims-2023-07-13/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">partial win</a> in its long legal tussle with the SEC, some crypto enthusiasts think the token’s price might finally hit $1 this year. The SEC contends that <a href=""/education/what-is-ripple-xrp/"">XRP</a> should be considered a security, which would put Ripple Labs (which issues XRP) under the SEC’s purview. However, in her summary judgment, the judge focused on Ripple’s marketing of the token instead. The SEC is <a href=""https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2023-08-18/sec-moves-to-appeal-ripple-ruling-that-crypto-is-not-a-security"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">appealing</a> the ruling.</p><p>The back-and-forth with the SEC was one of the reasons why the token didn’t participate in the November 2022 bull run. Nevertheless, the SEC lawsuit is a massive overhang on XRP’s price and how this plays out would ultimately dictate any upward price movement.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/XRP_price_0fb08c5a2f.jpg"" alt=""XRP price.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_XRP_price_0fb08c5a2f.jpg 202w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_XRP_price_0fb08c5a2f.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_XRP_price_0fb08c5a2f.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_XRP_price_0fb08c5a2f.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Ripple Labs' Legal Tussle With the SEC is a Major Overhang on its Price. Since inception, the token’s ROI stands at a whopping 8,623.91%.</p><h2>S&amp;P 500 vs. Top 10 Crypto Returns 2019-2022</h2><p>The S&amp;P 500 ended 2018 in the red, 2019, 2020 and 2021 with a bang, but it ended 2022 with a whimper.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/S_and_P_500_historial_data_c58bc146be.jpg"" alt=""S&amp;P 500 historical data"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_S_and_P_500_historial_data_c58bc146be.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_S_and_P_500_historial_data_c58bc146be.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_S_and_P_500_historial_data_c58bc146be.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>2022 Was a Bad Year for the S&amp;P 500 Index. Then, in the next three years, returns outpaced the average — 28.88%, 16.26% and 26.89% in 2019, 2020 and 2021, respectively, as everyone was hunkered indoors and the U.S. government handed free money as COVID-19 aid. But that’s where the trouble began.</p><p>The following year, the economy was red hot, leading to stubbornly high inflation, which forced the U.S. Federal Reserve to raise interest rates. The invasion of Ukraine, supply chain issues, and volatile economic data also kept markets on edge. All of this proved to be a perfect storm for the S&amp;P 500, which posted a return of -19.44% in 2022.</p><p>Cryptocurrencies aren’t insulated from macroeconomic factors with many coins having lost over 90% of their value, with many unlikely to recover, but major assets such as Bitcoin are suggesting that they may be able to weather bad news better than traditional asset classes like stocks.</p><h2>Performance of Top 10 Cryptos vs. S&amp;P 500 in 2023</h2><p>The research arm of megabank JPMorgan <a href=""https://www.jpmorgan.com/insights/research-mid-year-outlook#section-header#2"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">expects</a> a more challenging macro backdrop for stocks in the second half of 2023. Year to date, it is currently up about 14%. The return is, frankly, mediocre compared to a vast majority of top-10 crypto tokens. Let’s compare.</p><ul><li><strong>Bitcoin: </strong>The largest crypto is up 57.13% this year or $9,486.80.</li><li><strong>Ethereum:</strong> The second largest token has gained 37.76% year to date. In dollar value, that’s $453.11.</li><li><strong>BNB:</strong> Binance Coin is down 11.46% year to date.</li><li><strong>XRP:</strong> The token on the SEC’s radar is up 50.36% thus far in 2023.</li><li><strong>Cardano:</strong> The token ADA is up 5.13% in 2023.</li><li><strong>Dogecoin:</strong> Elon Musk’s favorite crypto is 11.30% in the red.</li><li><strong>Solana:</strong> SOL is down 34.83% over the preceding year.</li><li><strong>Tron: </strong>The token is up 40.14% year to date.</li></ul><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Bitcoin_10_Crypto_Index_Fund_0a62d47f28.jpg"" alt=""Bitcoin 10 Crypto Index Fund"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Bitcoin_10_Crypto_Index_Fund_0a62d47f28.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Bitcoin_10_Crypto_Index_Fund_0a62d47f28.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Bitcoin_10_Crypto_Index_Fund_0a62d47f28.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Bitcoin_10_Crypto_Index_Fund_0a62d47f28.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>The BitWise 10 Crypto Index Fund is up 44.1% Year to Date.
