Measures are:</p><ul style=""list-style-type:disc;""><li>SAFU (Secure Asset Funds) to reimburse users in the event of losses from a security breach.</li><li>Two-Factor authentication 2FA</li><li>Organizational Security</li><li>Proof of reserves (PoR)</li><li>Real-Time Monitoring</li><li>Security Notifications</li><li>Data Encryption</li><li>Secure Storage</li><li>IP Address Whitelisting</li><li>Withdrawal Address Whitelisting</li><li>API Whitelisting</li><li>Anti-Phishing Email Codes</li></ul><p><i><strong>Note:</strong> Users located in the US and UK are not supported.</i></p><h2>What is the Binance Exchange?</h2><p>Binance is the largest crypto exchange worldwide by the number of users and trading volume. The professional trading platform has low to zero fees, over 1,600 trading pairs, advanced trading options for experienced crypto traders and offers Binance users spot and derivative trading (some countries are restricted, so always check first).</p><p>Binance has an exceptional choice of ""Earn"" products, including DeFi staking, auto-invest, liquidity farming and Binance Pool.&nbsp;</p><p>Other notable features include the following: -</p><ul style=""list-style-type:disc;""><li><a href=""/review/binance-us-review/"">Binance US</a> (For US-Based Users)</li><li><a href=""/review/binance-app-review"">Mobile app</a></li><li>Crypto wallet</li><li><a href=""/review/binance/#binance-debit-card"">Crypto debit card</a></li><li>Institutional services</li><li>350+ cryptocurrencies</li><li>Over 1,600 trading markets</li><li>Fiat currency offramp services</li><li>More features and crypto products than most crypto exchanges</li></ul><h2>How Does Binance Secure Crypto?</h2><p>Not every crypto exchange takes care of account security as well as Binance. If you're <a href=""/education/cryptocurrency-beginners-guide/"">new to the crypto market</a>, you may wonder what would happen if the platform got hacked or some other catastrophic event caused the loss of your digital assets. Don't worry. In this section, you will learn the security measures Binance takes to protect your account.</p><h3>Binance Key Security Features</h3><p>Binance has several security features that contribute to protecting assets held on the platform by registered users.</p><h3>Safeguarding Your Funds: The Secure Asset Fund for Users (SAFU)</h3><p>In 2018, the Binance platform introduced a type of insurance fund referred to as the Secure Asset Fund for Users, or “SAFU” for short. The SAFU acts as an emergency reserve to protect user assets on the Binance platform. In the unlikely event that the platform gets hacked or anything causes users to lose digital assets (From Binance's perspective), the SAFU reimburses users.&nbsp;</p><p>The SAFU doesn't cover trading losses or any self-generated losses. For instance, it's your mistake if you lose your crypto wallet keys, mishandle your password, or cannot access your Binance account because you made a mistake. However, if a hacker gets your data or assets from a vulnerability in Binance's security systems, that is the responsibility of the platform to compensate your losses.&nbsp;</p><blockquote><p>""Binance stores 10% of all trading fees in a secure asset fund to protect a share of user funds."" (Source: Binance).</p></blockquote><h3>Two Factor Authentication</h3><p><a href=""https://staysafeonline.org/online-safety-privacy-basics/its-easy-to-stay-safe-online-with-these-4-steps-plus-1/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">2FA</a> isn't mandatory with Binance, but we highly recommend it as a security protocol. If someone accesses your password and you don't have 2FA enabled, you might only realize there was unauthorized access to your account when you log in and find your account balance is zero.</p><p>2FA acts as a stop measure, meaning that even if a hacker gets your password, they cannot access your account or make a withdrawal without also having access to your mobile device, which is also likely password-protected.</p><h3>Organizational Security</h3><p>Binance has several infrastructure features to ensure the integrity and safety of your funds (for the wallet and on the platform), including TSS (<a href=""https://eprint.iacr.org/2023/276"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">threshold signature schemes</a>), a cryptographic protocol for distributed key signing and distribution, and multisig (multiple signatures).</p><h3>Proof of Reserves (PoR)</h3><blockquote><p>""Binance has funds that cover all of our users assets 1:1, as well as some reserves."" (Source: <a href=""https://www.binance.com/en/proof-of-reserves"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Binance</a>).</p></blockquote><p>In February 2023, Binance became the first centralised crypto exchange (CEX) to implement <a href=""https://www.investopedia.com/terms/z/zksnark.asp"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">zk-SNARKS</a>, which are zero-knowledge protocols to increase the security and privacy of user data during verification.&nbsp;</p><p>In addition, Binance made the code open-source to further benefit the entire crypto industry security.</p><h3>Real-Time Monitoring</h3><p>Binance's risk management system analyses every 2FA&nbsp;or password reset, withdrawal attempt, and email address change. If it considers anything unusual happening, Binance suspends withdrawals for 24-48 hours or longer, depending on your responses.</p><p>Binance employs sophisticated round-the-clock monitoring systems to ensure that there is no unusual activity on the platform.</p><h3>Security Notifications</h3><p>You can help Binance protect your account by adjusting your settings to maximum security. The notifications could help prevent losses on your account from theft.</p><blockquote><p>""Secure From Day One: We safeguard user funds by securing our platform with strict protocols and industry-leading technical measures."" (Source: <a href=""https://www.binance.com/en/event/user_protection"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Binance</a>)</p></blockquote><h3>Data Encryption</h3><p>Binance uses end-to-end encryption for all transactions and encrypts your personal information and data in storage.&nbsp;</p><h3>Secure Storage</h3><p>Binance stores most client funds and assets in offline, <a href=""/review/cold-storage-ultimate-solution-crypto/"">cold storage facilities.</a></p><p>Considering an average day for Binance generates $38 billion in trading volume, the platform must operate dynamically with hot and cold wallets to provide real-time liquidity and, at the same time, mitigate potential security risks. It's a complex procedure to track real-time assets through its internal ledger, but every transaction is verifiable via the Binance PoR system (proof-of-reserves).</p><blockquote><p>""User assets are tracked entirely separately from Binance's corporate holdings."" (Source: <a href=""https://www.binance.com/en/blog/all/how-and-why-assets-move-between-binance-wallets-4835275628753556476"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Binance</a>)</p></blockquote><p>Moving funds between Binance wallets serves various purposes. It has to navigate transactions of all sizes, whether a significant withdrawal by a ""whale"" or an institution, which could cause chaos in liquidity if Binance fails to handle the transaction promptly and correctly.&nbsp;</p><p>The objective is to maintain liquidity and security by ensuring sufficient funds remain for platform trading liquidity and the remaining funds transfer to cold (offline) storage.</p><p>The below chart gives a step-by-step visual insight into how Binance moves user assets on the platform.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/binance_wallet_flow_ae62905193.jpg"" alt=""binance_wallet_flow.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_binance_wallet_flow_ae62905193.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_binance_wallet_flow_ae62905193.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_binance_wallet_flow_ae62905193.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_binance_wallet_flow_ae62905193.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>How Binance Manages The Flow Of Funds For Deposits: Image Source: Binance</figcaption></figure><p>Periodically, Binance consolidates by transferring funds from deposit wallets into ""omnibus hot wallets."" This process helps Binance meet user withdrawal requests and minimise costs and wait times.</p><blockquote><p>""Excess funds are moved from hot wallets to safe storage in cold or offline wallets. We refer to this process as overflow. Once a hot wallet runs low on funds, it might need a top-up from a cold wallet."" (Source: <a href=""https://www.binance.com/en/blog/all/how-and-why-assets-move-between-binance-wallets-4835275628753556476"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Binance</a>)</p></blockquote><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/binance_flow_0a27e2a9e8.jpg"" alt=""binance-flow.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_binance_flow_0a27e2a9e8.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_binance_flow_0a27e2a9e8.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_binance_flow_0a27e2a9e8.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_binance_flow_0a27e2a9e8.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>How Binance Manages The Flow of Withdrawals: Image Source: Binance</figcaption></figure><p>So, we've established that Binance takes significant measures to safeguard the platform, but let's discover what you can do to help take care of your digital assets.</p><h2>How to Secure Your Cryptocurrency Exchange Account on Binance</h2><p>Binance is excellent at providing a range of security options, but it helps if you also take measures to protect your account.</p><p>When you open a Binance account, you can restrict addresses to prevent devices from accessing your account. We recommend setting up personalised access control from the start. Whitelisting wallets and IP addresses help to protect your account.</p><p>Binance encourages safe sign-in protocols, such as 2FA, including SMS, email, hardware and app-based. Due to what is known as a <a href=""https://www.kaspersky.com/resource-center/threats/sim-swapping"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Sim-Swap attack</a>, most security professionals do not recommend using SMS, but opt for the more secure 2FA such as Google Authenticator or Authy on your mobile device or using a dedicated 2FA device like YubiKey.</p><p>It's advisable to use a super strong password along with a password manager. Use lower and upper case, digits and special characters. If you cannot remember your password without writing it down, that's a positive sign you have nailed a strong password, hence where a password manager can save the day.</p><p>Avoid using a generic password like Brian1234 or one you regularly use for other accounts.&nbsp;</p><p>By enabling notifications in your security settings, you can opt-in to receive security notifications from the Binance support team for login attempts. This can help identify if someone tries to get into your account pretending to be you.</p><p>Adding multiple layers to your account security is always a good plan.</p><blockquote><p>""Binance maintains completely separate ledgers for user funds, pegged assets, and its own holdings. At any given moment, we know exactly how much money each of our users is entitled to, and we hold sufficient funds to honor any withdrawal request. And, again, it's all verifiable via the PoR system."" (Source: <a href=""https://www.binance.com/en/blog/all/how-and-why-assets-move-between-binance-wallets-4835275628753556476"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Binance</a>)</p></blockquote><h2>Binance Wallet Security</h2><p>You can choose Binance's <a href=""/review/trust-wallet/"">Trust Wallet</a>, a popular self-custody wallet with over 60 million users, or use the Binance Wallet Chrome extension if you want to stick with Binance-approved self-custody wallet solutions.&nbsp;</p><p>As with other exchanges, Binance users have two choices: They can either keep their funds on the Binance Exchange or withdraw their assets to a self-custodial wallet. Most security-minded crypto users would highly recommend withdrawing any funds from an exchange that you don't intend to trade. You can find out why along with other crypto safety best practices in our <a href=""/education/crypto-safety-protect-crypto/"">Crypto Safety Guidelines</a> article.</p><p>Trust Wallet is a fantastic choice for mobile crypto wallets, but if you want the most secure crypto storage wallets available, you may want to check out our article on the <a href=""/analysis/best-hardware-wallets/"">Top Hardware Wallets</a>.</p><p>Regardless of the wallet you choose, always choose a strong password combining letters, capital and lowercase, digits and special characters. If you can opt-in for biometric access, all the better, as nobody has your face or fingerprints.&nbsp;</p><p>When setting up your wallet, write the seed phase somewhere safe and secure. Without this recovery phase, you could permanently lose access to your wallet. (We cover this in detail in the Crypto Safety Guidelines article above)</p><p>2FA might seem a pain when you want to access your wallet fast, but it's extra security for stopping others from fast access to your crypto holdings.&nbsp;</p><h2>Binance Mobile App Security</h2><p>The same rules apply to the <a href=""/review/binance-app-review/"">Binance mobile app</a> as to a crypto wallet. We've all become blasé about using our phones in public and trusting security, but our relaxed approach to trading or buying crypto on mobile apps can be dangerous.&nbsp;</p><p>After you download the Binance mobile app, consider the following 8 security tips: -</p><ol><li>Install reputable antivirus protection that offers passcode app locking.</li><li>Update your phone regularly.</li><li>Install a 2FA authenticator such as Google Authenticator or Authy.</li><li>Lock the Binance app if possible.</li><li>Have a lock screen password on your phone, so nobody can access the apps, even if you lose your mobile.</li><li>Consider <a href=""https://go.coinbureau.com/expressvpn"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener nofollow"">installing a VPN</a> for added encrypted security.</li><li>Ideally, don't use the Binance mobile app using public WiFi.</li></ol><p>It might seem a hassle to consider implementing extra security, but protecting your crypto assets is a priority if you want to stay in the crypto market for the long term.</p><h2>Binance vs. Binance US</h2><p>After the United States cracked down on crypto rules and regulations, US regulators classified many Binance assets as ""securities"", part of a financial category including futures, stocks and bonds. As a result, Binance created a US-specific platform for traders and crypto investors based in the United States called <a href=""/review/binance-us-review/"">Binance US</a>.</p><p>Customer support is still 24/7 via email and online chat.</p><p>Although Binance US is available to most states, it is not available to Hawaii, Texas, New York and Vermont. Binance is working to implement compliance requirements globally, as are many cryptocurrency exchanges.&nbsp;</p><p>Fees, trading, and minimum deposit ($10) are the same, and both platforms support desktop, mobile and web trading.</p><p>Binance US supports USD, EUR and AUD, among others, and over 120 cryptocurrencies. You can read our <a href=""/review/binance-vs-binance-us-review/"">Binance vs. Binance US</a> review for a more detailed comparison.&nbsp;</p><p>In conclusion, besides less liquidity, fewer services, and the method of customer support, Binance and Binance US both prioritise user account security and customer fund security, so the same guidelines apply throughout this article.</p><h2>So, Is Binance Safe?</h2><p>We began this article by asking, ""Is Binance safe?"" Of course, the definition of safe can be subject to individual perspectives. Our objective was to determine if depositing funds with Binance is secure, using the trading platform safely and withdrawing cryptos to your wallet.&nbsp;</p><p>In addition, we looked at the security of the Binance mobile wallet and app.</p><p>Whilst we always encourage you to adopt a <a href=""/education/crypto-safety-protect-crypto/"">responsible approach to securing your digital assets</a>, Binance provides a good selection of tools to help you do so. The peace of mind from knowing Binance has a SAFU in place is a big bonus.&nbsp;</p><p>In November 2022, as the crypto market plunged, Changpeng Zhao (CZ) topped up the Binance SAFU to $1 billion to provide additional security to Binance users during the challenging bear market. In his tweet, Changpeng stated that BNB and BUSD accounted for $700 million and $300 million for the BTC address.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Binance_SAFU_da5619c181.jpg"" alt=""Binance_SAFU.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Binance_SAFU_da5619c181.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Binance_SAFU_da5619c181.jpg 500w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>In November 2022, Binance CEO Changpeng Zhao announced a SAFU Top Up to $1 Billion: Image Source: <a href=""https://twitter.com/cz_binance/status/1596024145686716416?lang=en"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">CZ Binance Twitter</a></figcaption></figure><p>In recent years, regulators worldwide have accused Binance of compliance issues and not responding to requests to provide essential information. It's tricky to get a clear picture as most of it has been mere hearsay, and many in the crypto community feel it is nothing more than a witch hunt amidst the ongoing <a href=""https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=tV1jp4FrKlU"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Chokepoint 2.0</a>, but it is important to note that these accusations against Binance do exist. However, as Binance has over 150 million users worldwide and is by far, the largest crypto exchange in the world, they're clearly doing a lot right by its customers.&nbsp;</p><p>Trust Wallet and the Binance Wallet Chrome extension are popular self-custody wallets downloaded by millions of users. If you follow the guidelines for protecting your digital assets, either wallet is acceptable. OKX lacks this feature which is why many crypto users will still use an exchange like Crypto.com, Kraken, or Binance to deposit funds, then simply transfer crypto to OKX to take advantage of the exchange.</p><ul><li><strong>Full-featured platform</strong></li></ul><p>As mentioned in the Pros section, the OKX app has a huge selection of advanced crypto trading products and features available, which can be a double-edged sword.</p><p>While the OKX app is user-friendly and beginners can quickly get the hang of it, the fact that OKX is suitable for advanced traders as well as features a huge range of crypto products means that there are plenty of functions, features, and entire areas of the app that new traders may find overwhelming, making it not the most beginner-friendly crypto trading app.&nbsp;</p><p>The app can feel quite confusing for new users with all sorts of features and settings that many of us will never use. If you are looking for a simple no-frills crypto app, I would recommend <a href=""/review/swissborg-chsb/"">SwissBorg</a> or Kraken as being the most beginner-friendly.</p><p>Fortunately though, to try and combat this, users can easily switch between Lite, Web3, and Pro modes to help make it easier for new users not needing all the bells and whistles.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/OKX_pro_5d43a705a5.jpg"" alt=""OKX pro"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_OKX_pro_5d43a705a5.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_OKX_pro_5d43a705a5.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_OKX_pro_5d43a705a5.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_OKX_pro_5d43a705a5.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Image via OKX</figcaption></figure><h2>User Experience with OKX App</h2><p>The user experience with the OKX app is generally positive among the community according to reviews and Twitter/Reddit statements. After using the app myself, I found the app to be well-designed and easy to navigate. While I don’t typically use mobile apps for frequent trading due to the small screen and lack of additional monitors and research tools, (I go into more detail on why traders don’t use mobile apps in our <a href=""/review/coinbase-pro/"">Coinbase Review</a>), the app does have a suitable range of trading tools and features that make it easier for traders to manage their portfolios on the go.</p><p>I found the app served its purpose well of being able to keep an eye on your portfolio, manage open positions, and for the odd time you do need to place a trade while away from a computer. The app also gives users the ability to:</p><ul><li>Trade Spot, Margin, and <a href=""https://www.stlouisfed.org/publications/regional-economist/october-1994/demystifying-derivatives"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Derivatives</a></li><li>Access Lite and Pro versions on the same app</li><li>Buy crypto with card</li><li>Access the P2P exchange</li><li>Access <a href=""/review/okx-earn/"">Earn</a> to benefit from DeFi and earn passive income on your crypto.&nbsp;</li><li>Utilize <a href=""/review/okx-trading-bots/"">OKX Trading Bots</a></li><li>Get crypto insights and alerts on the go</li><li>Use the analysis feature to view the profit and loss (PnL) performance trend for your portfolio over a daily, monthly, or self-selected period. Users can gain insights to help manage investment portfolios in the areas of finance, data analytics, pool mining, and cryptocurrency wallets.</li></ul><p>However, I should mention that some users have reported issues with the app's stability, and trade execution, particularly during times of high trading volume. These complaints are not common and may have had something to do with the trader’s network connection as opposed to the app itself, and I have never personally encountered any connectivity issues.</p><p>I have had issues with frequent redesigns of the apps where certain features and functions have moved or disappeared. One of my favourite features was that there used to be Satoshi giveaways for daily logins and a simple betting feature where you’d bet Satoshis whether you thought the price of BTC would go up or down in the next 24 hours. Those features disappeared without warning, which was a bummer, so I would also warn about not becoming too attached to some functions of the app as they may randomly disappear one day 😡</p><h2>Security Measures of the OKX App</h2><p>OKX takes security seriously, the app has a range of security measures in place to protect users' funds. The app uses two-factor authentication (2FA) and passwords to secure user accounts, takes advantage of mobile biometrics security, and also has a range of other security features, such as SSL encryption and cold storage for user funds.</p><p>The OKX approach to security and cold storage solutions is actually one of the most robust I’ve seen in the industry and I have long been impressed by the security measures and protocols in place. I won’t go into detail here as we cover it in our dedicated <a href=""/review/okx/"">OKX review</a>. You can also take a look at their multi-pronged approach to security on their&nbsp;<a href=""https://www.okx.com/wallet-security"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Security Page</a>.</p><h2>Comparison with Other Trading Apps</h2><p>Compared to other cryptocurrency trading apps, the OKX app has some advantages and disadvantages. When compared to Coinbase, the OKX app has a far wider range of cryptocurrencies and more advanced trading features. However, Coinbase has better customer support, benefits from a stronger reputation, is regulated, and is more beginner friendly.&nbsp;</p><p>A note on Coinbase though, it is great for beginners, but I have found it quite common for many traders to “outgrow” Coinbase and move onto an exchange such as OKX, <a href=""/review/bitget-exchange-review/"">Bitget</a>, or Binance to access the lower fees and more trading functionality, as well as a better selection of crypto products like staking, earn, crypto borrowing, lending, and more.</p><p>When compared to Binance, the OKX app has better security measures and access to the Web3 Wallet, but Binance has a wider range of payment options and better fiat on and off-ramp support. SwissBorg might be the easiest to use and one of the most unique crypto apps around. SwissBorg is not suitable for trading with technical analysis, as there is no charting functionality, but the platform aggregates low-fee swaps from many leading exchanges to provide users with simple one-click trading. SwissBorg is also more of a crypto wealth management platform as opposed to a trading exchange like OKX. I have used OKX in the past and found their support to be adequate, and for the purpose of this review, I tested their support response times over a span of 3 days, messaging in at different times of the day with a mix of simple and complex answers.</p><p><a href=""https://guy.coinbureau.com/signup/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Newsletter_inline_a4c7553089.jpg"" alt=""Newsletter Inline"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Newsletter_inline_a4c7553089.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Newsletter_inline_a4c7553089.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Newsletter_inline_a4c7553089.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""></a></p><p>I found I received responses within a minute or two in most cases, with some of the more complex questions taking over ten minutes so they could track down the answer. (Source: Tron)</p></blockquote><h2>Tron TRX Summary</h2><figure class=""table""><table><tbody><tr><td>Throughput/TPS</td><td>2,000 TPS compared to 15 TPS Ethereum and 7 Bitcoin TPS</td></tr><tr><td>TRON Virtual Machine (TVM)&nbsp;</td><td>TVM is the runtime environment for TRON smart contracts. Each node in the network maintains a TVM entity</td></tr><tr><td>Governed By</td><td>The Tron Foundation</td></tr><tr><td>Native Cryptocurrency</td><td>TRON (TRX)&nbsp;</td></tr><tr><td>Consensus Mechanism</td><td>Delegated Proof of Stake (DPOS)</td></tr><tr><td>Smart Contract Functionality</td><td>TRON supports the execution of smart contracts written in programming languages like Solidity and Java, making it more accessible to developers.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>Smart contracts enable the creation of DApps on the TRON network</td></tr><tr><td>Transaction Fees</td><td>From Zero</td></tr><tr><td>Registered Users</td><td>160+ million</td></tr><tr><td>Founded</td><td>2017</td></tr><tr><td>Location</td><td>Singapore</td></tr></tbody></table></figure><p><strong>Tron TRX Review: Summary&nbsp;</strong></p><p>Tron (TRX) is a decentralised blockchain launched in 2017 and developed by the Tron Foundation. Tron's goal was to become a more efficient layer-one blockchain than existing networks, and have enjoyed a level of success in terms of developer activity and adoption.</p><p><strong>The Key Features of Tron are:</strong></p><p>Tron has three core features: -</p><ol style=""list-style-type:decimal;""><li><strong>High-Throughput:</strong> The TRONPROTOCOL has fast transaction speeds of 2,000 TPS.</li><li><strong>High-Scalability:</strong> The TRONPROTOCOL can accommodate a large user base, and smart contracts enable diverse ways of deploying smart contracts.</li><li><strong>High-Availability:</strong> The TRONPROTOCOL has intrinsic value, a robust and reliable network structure, and user assets. The decentralised proof of stake (DPoS) enables an effective rewards distribution system.</li></ol><p><a href=""/deals/trading/bitget-crypto-exchange/""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Bitget_Deals_CTA_3581081c63.jpg"" alt=""Bitget-Deals-CTA.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Bitget_Deals_CTA_3581081c63.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Bitget_Deals_CTA_3581081c63.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Bitget_Deals_CTA_3581081c63.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_Bitget_Deals_CTA_3581081c63.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""></a></p><h2>A Brief History of Tron</h2><h3>Who Created Tron and Why?</h3><p>Tron (TRX) is a blockchain launched in 2017 and developed by the Tron Foundation to create a decentralised internet. The CEO, Justin Sun, initially deployed TRX tokens (ERC-20) on the <a href=""https://ethereum.org/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Ethereum</a> network but later moved away. It was probably a decision that determined the success of the project.</p><figure class=""image image_resized"" style=""width:75%;""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/justin_sun_e243566f4e_1a4d008de7.webp"" alt=""justin_sun_e243566f4e.webp"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_justin_sun_e243566f4e_1a4d008de7.webp 156w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Justin Sun, Tron CEO and a 30 under 30 Entrepreneur: Image Source Forbes</figcaption></figure><p>The Tron Foundation launched the project intending to give ownership rights to content creators, notably for digital content. Content creators can connect directly with their audience, which allows them to maximise and monetise content more efficiently.</p><p>If we consider how we stream content via the leading tech giants, it's an unfair system. For example, YouTube can randomly decide to close a user's account and choose to censor certain content while promoting others.</p><p>Facebook can decrease reach or, worse, ban the content creator from posting or commenting in their group. Come on, Mark Zuckerberg, do you genuinely think your big-boy micromanaging approach is fair to your users?&nbsp;</p><p>The problem is we do not own our content. Content creators, like musicians, struggle to make a living when the streaming tech giants like Spotify and Apple stomp all over uploaded content with an ""<i>it's mine now""&nbsp;</i>attitude. They pay content creators a few peanuts for their work whilst they make the lion's share for doing, well, not much at all, other than being ""big.""&nbsp;</p><p>You know what I am talking about.</p><p>For this reason, Tron sought to become a disruptor in an unbalanced playing field. You, me, and content creators worldwide should be glad about that, and the tech giants should watch their backs and not rest on their considerable laurels.</p><h3>What is the TRON Network</h3><p>Tron supports <a href=""/analysis/best-tron-dapps/"">dApps</a>, smart contracts and numerous blockchain systems. It uses the <a href=""https://blockonomi.com/utxo-vs-account-based-transaction-models/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">account-based</a> model , a transaction model similar to <a href=""/education/what-is-ethereum"">Ethereum</a>, with a transparent public ledger for anyone to track transaction history. Anyone can build and develop dApps on the Tron network, and if users provide and share their content, Tron rewards them with digital assets.</p><p>The TRON ecosystem includes a blockchain explorer, lending platforms, DEXes, wallets, and even a decentralised oracle.</p><p>Many of the talent team on Tron are highly experienced individuals from projects such as <a href=""/press-release/brd-strategic-partnership-ripple/"">Ripple</a> Labs.&nbsp;</p><blockquote><p>""Since TRON DAO was founded, it has upheld its original faith of decentralizing the Internet, working hard to change the world with technology."" (Source: Tron)</p></blockquote><h3>What is Tron's Technology?</h3><p>Tron adapts a 3-layer architecture divided into Storage Layer, Core Layer, and Application Layer. The TRON protocol adheres to Google Protobuf, which intrinsically supports the multi-language extension. (Source: Tron&nbsp;<a href=""https://tron.network/static/doc/white_paper_v_2_0.pdf"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Whitepaper</a>).</p><p>Tron's stack-based virtual machine (<a href=""https://tronscan-org.medium.com/tronscan-class-tron-virtual-machine-tvm-d007dc194ffe"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">TVM</a>) has an optimised instruction set. <a href=""/smart-contracts/want-learn-solidity-dapp/"">Solidity </a>is the smart contract programming language for dApp developers.</p><p>The TVM connects with development systems to provide a custom-built, secure, stable, and efficient blockchain system for developers worldwide.</p><h3>How does the TRON Network Work?</h3><p>The Tron network uses a <a href=""https://www.techopedia.com/definition/33597/delegated-proof-of-stake-dpos"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">delegated proof-of-stake</a> (DPoS) consensus mechanism. Tron users vote for “super representatives” (SRs) who earn fees by validating network transactions. Due to the decentralised nature, the Tron users have governance on the network, and nobody has control over more than one network node.</p><p><strong>Tron uses a 3-layer architecture: -</strong></p><ol><li>Core</li><li>Storage</li><li>Application</li></ol><p>This architecture helps reduce the typical latency associated with more conventional networks and the high transaction costs.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/TVM_workflow_37773ddd6c.jpg"" alt=""TVM_workflow.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_TVM_workflow_37773ddd6c.jpg 144w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_TVM_workflow_37773ddd6c.jpg 461w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Tron's TVM Workflow: Image Source Tron <a href=""https://tron.network/static/doc/white_paper_v_2_0.pdf"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Whitepaper</a></figcaption></figure><h2>What is Tron (TRX)?</h2><p>The Tron (TRX) token is for rewarding users for creating and sharing content such as music, videos and photos. TRX is also used for online gaming as a currency, for powering lending platforms and decentralised exchanges.</p><p>Tron is an open-source project using permissionless protocols and tools to deliver global content to its users and, additionally, TRX is used for smart contract-based financial projects.</p><p>TRX holders have governance on the network.&nbsp;</p><h3>Tron’s Periander Upgrade</h3><p>In July 2023, Tron released Great Voyage v4.7.2 (Periander), an upgraded version of its mainnet. The upgrade introduced significant improvements in four areas:</p><p><strong>Advanced stake 2.0 mechanism</strong></p><p>Two important governance proposals for TRON stake 2.0 are part of the upgrade. The first proposal allows users to withdraw their unstaking requests that are still in progress. The second proposal empowers users to customize the lockup period for delegated resources according to their individual needs.</p><p><strong>Compatibility with Ethereum's EIP-3855</strong></p><p>This new governance proposal ensures the compatibility between Tron and Ethereum's virtual machines while reducing the associated costs to deploy and use smart contracts on the Tron network. The company hopes this will attract more developers to and promote enhanced interoperability between Tron and Ethereum ecosystems.</p><p><strong>Streamlined smart contract interface calling</strong></p><p>As part of this upgrade, Tron has optimized triggersmartcontract and triggerconstantcontract, two interfaces for calling smart contracts, to provide developers with estimated transaction fees for deploying their contracts. Tron said this paves the way for the creation of more high-quality DApps.</p><p><strong>Revamped P2P network module</strong></p><p>Four key functionalities were introduced:</p><ul><li>The upgraded network now incorporates a pre-detection mechanism for nodes pending connection to filter out invalid connection requests.</li><li>The implementation of the DNS protocol improves the platform's availability by enabling the discovery of active nodes that are ready to connect to the Tron network.</li><li>The network now supports the IPv6 protocol, a crucial development that enhances the scalability of Java-tron's network architecture in the future.</li><li>The introduction of message compression before transmission reduces the bandwidth requirements for Java-tron, leading to lower operational and maintenance costs.</li></ul><h2>How Do You Get Free Tron (TRX) Transaction Fees?</h2><p>Are Tron (TRX) transaction fees really free? Well, they can be.</p><blockquote><p>""TRON network generally does not charge fees for most transactions; however, due to system restrictions and fairness, bandwidth usage and transactions do take in certain fees."" (Source: Tron)</p></blockquote><ol><li>Tron issues 5,000 FREE bandwidth points daily to users. You can freeze TRX to get more bandwidth points if you need more. The amount of TRX required is the number of bytes (10 SUN: 1 TRX = 1,000,000 SUN: <i>See below for an explanation of&nbsp;</i>SUN).</li><li>Smart contracts use ""energy"" and require bandwidth points for broadcasting and confirming transactions.</li><li>Query transactions are FREE, as no energy or bandwidth is required.</li></ol><p>TRON network also defines a set of fixed fees for the following transactions:</p><ul style=""list-style-type:disc;""><li>Creating a witness node: 9999 TRX</li><li>Issuing a TRC-10 token: 1024 TRX</li><li>Creating a new account: 0.1 TRX</li><li>Creating an exchange pair: 1024 TRX</li></ul><p>(Source: Tron <a href=""https://tron.network/static/doc/white_paper_v_2_0.pdf"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Whitepaper</a>)</p><p>Tron (TRX) transactions are exceptionally low compared to other crypto networks. For example, you could pay hundreds of dollars in transaction fees on the <a href=""https://ethereum.org/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Ethereum</a> (ETH) network.</p><h3>What is The Sun Network?</h3><blockquote><p>""SUN's main purpose is to exist as support for the TRON protocol, which aims to create a decentralized internet ecosystem. SUN specifically focuses on DeFi and aiding its uptake and infiltration on TRON's blockchain."" (Source: CoinMarketCap)</p></blockquote><h2>TRX Price and Potential</h2><p>You would have been hiding under a rock not to know we've been in a crypto bear market for a good while.&nbsp;</p><p>In June 2022, Tron (TRX) was at a high of $0.0806 when it suddenly dropped below $0.0602. (2023),Review,"<p>When you're new to <a href=""/education/cryptocurrency-beginners-guide/"">cryptocurrencies</a>, one of the biggest challenges you face is choosing a cryptocurrency exchange you can trust. Of course, every crypto enthusiast has their favourites, usually based on personal experience. Still, the essential component is whether an exchange offers the security, products, and services you need. In addition, a record of customer service should also count in your decision.</p><p><a href=""/review/gemini"">Gemini </a>and Kraken are reputable, established, USA-based cryptocurrency exchanges. Gemini began in 2014. The Winklevoss twins, Tyler and Cameron, opened the launch with a determined focus on security first and quickly became one of the most regulated and compliant crypto exchanges worldwide.</p><p><a href=""/review/kraken"">Kraken</a> is one of the largest crypto exchanges popular with beginners, advanced traders, and investors. Established in 2011 by Jesse Powell and owned by Payward.Inc, Kraken was among the first to offer users access to derivatives, spot trading and index products.</p><p>In this Gemini vs Kraken article, we will look at two of the top cryptocurrency exchanges suitable for all levels of investors and traders. Hopefully, you will soon know if either of these companies is right for you.</p><p>We intend to look at each exchange individually, but below is a quick overview of our findings by comparing Gemini and Kraken.</p><h2>Gemini vs Kraken: Products Offered</h2><h3>Gemini Products</h3><p>Gemini has an excellent range of services that appeal to all levels of traders and investors.</p><ul><li><strong>Web Trader: </strong>A beginner-friendly platform for retail traders. It's an easy interface to navigate if you're just starting in crypto trading</li><li><strong>ActiveTrader:</strong> Once you have some trading experience under your belt, Active Trader is the next step. You must request access to this service. Once you have permission, you can place the following orders:&nbsp;<ul><li><strong>Limit Order: </strong>A pre-placed buy or sell order to execute at a predetermined price.</li><li><strong>Market Order: </strong>An immediate live buy or sell order to the market.</li><li><strong>Maker-or-Cancel:</strong> An order executed (only) if it gets you the ""maker"" fee.</li><li><strong>Immediate-or-Cancel (IOC):</strong> It will execute part or all of your order.</li><li><strong>Fill-or-Kill (FOC): </strong>Immediate order execution. You cannot do partial orders</li></ul></li><li><strong>Auction</strong>: A daily auction (inc holidays and weekends) for Gemini's listed cryptocurrencies. To engage, switch to ""Daily Auction"" from the ActiveTrader interface.</li><li><strong>Block Trade: </strong>Liquidity can be affected by large orders coming into the market, which can cause slippage issues. Placing a block trade order is like an OTC (over-the-counter) service.</li><li><strong>Gemini Earn: </strong>Earn a small yield from your crypto whilst you aren't using it. The small interest rates won't pay the mortgage, but every bit helps, right?</li><li><strong>Gemini Clearing: </strong>This service enables two parties to trade directly and anonymously. Gemini acts as a trusted third party.</li><li><strong>Gemini Mobile: </strong>You can use the mobile app (for iOS and Android) with Web Trader but not ActiveTrader.</li></ul><p>So, I'm sure you will agree that <a href=""/review/gemini"">Gemini&nbsp;</a>has an impressive product range, so now let's look at Krakens products.</p><p><a href=""/deals/wallet/unstoppable-domains/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener nofollow""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/Unstoppable_Domains_Inline_f1d93210d7.jpg"" alt=""Unstoppable Domains Inline"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_Unstoppable_Domains_Inline_f1d93210d7.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_Unstoppable_Domains_Inline_f1d93210d7.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_Unstoppable_Domains_Inline_f1d93210d7.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""></a></p><h3>Kraken Products</h3><p>After registration and account verification, you can access Kraken via the web platform or, if you prefer, download the Kraken app (available for Android and iOS).</p><ul><li><strong>Staking: </strong>No matter what's happening in the crypto market, you can earn up to 23% with popular PoS (<a href=""/analysis/proof-of-work-vs-proof-of-stake/"">proof-of-stake</a>) crypto assets listed with Kraken.&nbsp;</li><li><strong>Crypto Education:</strong> Kraken Learn is a superb service to help educate you on everything crypto. The video, webinars, crypto guides, and podcasts provide in-depth information and can only help you learn how to maximise your financial understanding of cryptocurrencies.</li><li><strong>Kraken App: </strong>Kraken has two mobile apps. One is for advanced trading, and the other is for day-to-day trading and hodling.<ul><li><strong>Kraken Pro: </strong>This app has an easy and attractive interface. It is super easy to navigate, even for beginners. You can execute, monitor and adjust trades on the go.</li><li><strong>Kraken App: </strong>With over 1M downloads, the Kraken app is popular with users for tracking, converting, buying, and selling cryptocurrencies listed with Kraken. It has low fees, exceptional security (biometric &amp; password protected), 24/7 support, and multiple payment options.&nbsp;</li></ul></li><li><strong>Kraken Pro:</strong> For more advanced traders, the Kraken Pro platform offers lower fees than the standard platform, more suitable for beginners. You gain access to more order types, charting, and tools for advanced trading.</li></ul><p>Kraken may not have as many products as Gemini, but it has an excellent reputation for providing a good service for its users and is often considered the most secure exchange in the industry.</p><h2>Gemini vs Kraken: User Friendliness</h2><p>In the early days, navigating the user interface on most cryptocurrency exchanges was like dropping an alien in the middle of London and asking it to find a specific street (from over 40,000). Buying, selling and <a href=""/education/cryptocurrency-beginners-guide/"">trading cryptocurrencies </a>was so complex it repelled many new users from adopting cryptocurrencies and changing their finances.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>Thankfully, times have changed. Gemini and Kraken are user-friendly with easy-to-navigate interfaces. Still, are there differences between the two, and if so, what are they?</p><p>Gemini and Kraken have iOS and Android mobile apps for trading and managing your crypto portfolio. Of the two, Gemini has the slight advantage of user-friendliness, as it is a bit easier for beginners to navigate the interface. In addition, the AutoTrader option is ideal for more advanced traders. Gemini also has multiple guides to help support crypto newbies.</p><p><a href=""/review/kraken"">Kraken</a> is a user-friendly platform but leans slightly towards a more advanced user, especially with Kraken Pro. It's not quite as intuitive as Gemini's interface. However, finding your way around Kraken's website and trading platforms is not challenging once you familiarise yourself with how it works.</p><p>Both crypto exchanges are suitable for all levels of traders and investors. Still, if you are new to cryptocurrency exchanges, anticipate a bit more of a learning curve with Kraken.</p><h2>Gemini vs Kraken: Fees</h2><p>Both Kraken and Gemini have competitive fees. Though the breakdown can seem a little complex, it isn't once you understand how the fee structure works.</p><h3>Deposit and Withdrawal Fees</h3><p>You can deposit most fiat currencies for free with Kraken. Withdrawal fees vary depending on what currency you are withdrawing. There is a minimum withdrawal fee and a flat fee for transactions when moving your funds from your Kraken account.</p><p>Deposit fees for Kraken are variable, but some crypto deposits incur variable on-chain costs, such as <a href=""https://ethereum.org/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Ethereum </a>and Ethereum Classic. Terra Classic and TerraUSD Classic deposits incur a 0.2% tax burn.</p><p>Wire deposits and bank transfers are free with <a href=""/review/gemini"">Gemini</a>, but check transfer fees from your bank. You can deposit with a debit or credit card with fiat currencies, but there is a 3.49% fee, and this service is not available to United States users.</p><p>Each month, Gemini allows you to have up to ten crypto withdrawals for free, which you cannot roll over into the next month.&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>Trading Fees</p><p>Both exchanges base fee structures on 30-day trading volume at variable levels.</p><h3>Gemini Web &amp; Mobile Trading Fees (Standard)</h3><ul><li>Less than $10.00 = $0.99&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>$10.00 to less than $25.00 = $1.49&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>$25.00 to less than $50.00 = $1.99&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>$50.00 to less than $200 = $2.99&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>$200+ = 1.49% of the order value</li></ul><h3>Gemini Maker &amp; Taker &amp; Fees</h3><figure class=""table""><table><tbody><tr><td>30-Day Volume Maker Taker</td><td>Maker</td><td>Taker</td></tr><tr><td>$0&nbsp;</td><td>&nbsp;0.40%&nbsp;</td><td>0.20%</td></tr><tr><td>$10,000</td><td>0.30%</td><td>&nbsp; 0.10%</td></tr><tr><td>$50,000</td><td>0.25%</td><td>&nbsp; 0.10%</td></tr><tr><td>$100,000</td><td>&nbsp;0.20%</td><td>&nbsp;0.08%</td></tr><tr><td>$1,000,000&nbsp;</td><td>0.15%</td><td>&nbsp;0.05%</td></tr><tr><td>$5,000,000</td><td>&nbsp;0.10%</td><td>&nbsp;0.03%</td></tr><tr><td>$10,000</td><td>&nbsp;0.08%</td><td>0.02%</td></tr></tbody></table></figure><h3><br>Kraken Maker &amp; Taker Fees</h3><blockquote><p><i>""Kraken fees for buying, selling, or converting assets using Instant Buy consists of a displayed fee and, where applicable, a spread which is included in the price. Any spread is calculated before orders are executed and may differ for similar transactions because the spread is determined based on a combination of factors, including but not limited to transaction size, asset, payment method and market conditions.""</i>&nbsp;&nbsp;<br><i>(Source: Kraken)</i></p></blockquote><figure class=""table""><table><tbody><tr><td>30-Day Volume&nbsp;</td><td>Maker</td><td>Taker</td></tr><tr><td>$0 - $50,000&nbsp;</td><td>0.16%&nbsp;</td><td>0.26%</td></tr><tr><td>$50,001 - $100,000</td><td>&nbsp;0.14%&nbsp;</td><td>0.24%</td></tr><tr><td>$100,001 - $250,000</td><td>&nbsp;0.12%&nbsp;</td><td>0.22%</td></tr><tr><td>$250,001 - $500,000</td><td>&nbsp;0.10%&nbsp;</td><td>0.20%</td></tr><tr><td>$500,001 - $1,000,000</td><td>&nbsp;0.08%&nbsp;</td><td>0.18%</td></tr><tr><td>$1,000,001 - $2,500,00&nbsp;</td><td>0.06%&nbsp;</td><td>0.16%</td></tr><tr><td>$2,500,001 – $5,000,000&nbsp;</td><td>0.04%&nbsp;</td><td>0.14%</td></tr><tr><td>$5,000,001 - $10,000,000 &nbsp;</td><td>0.02%</td><td>0.12%</td></tr><tr><td>$10,000,000+&nbsp;</td><td>0.00%&nbsp;</td><td>0.10%</td></tr></tbody></table></figure><h2>Gemini vs Kraken: Security</h2><p>From the offset, Gemini determined security as a priority. They take it very seriously indeed. From asset protection, user account management, internal control, and compliance, Gemini stands above many leading crypto exchanges for its attention to security.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/shutterstock_2122606175_13831fca25.jpg"" alt=""Gemini Takes Security Seriously"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_shutterstock_2122606175_13831fca25.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_shutterstock_2122606175_13831fca25.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_shutterstock_2122606175_13831fca25.jpg 750w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Gemini Prioritises Account Security. Image Source: Shutterstock</figcaption></figure><p><strong>The following are some of the security measures taken to protect your Gemini account and digital assets: -</strong></p><ul><li>2FA (two-factor authentication).</li><li>Support for hardware security keys.</li><li>Whitelisted withdrawal addresses.</li><li>Gemini stores most crypto assets in <a href=""/analysis/bitcoin-multisignature-wallets/"">multisig</a> (multiple signatures required for access) <a href=""/education/how-do-hardware-wallets-work/"">cold wallets</a>.</li><li>Gemini's HSMS (hardware security modules) are ""FIPS 140-2 Level 3 rating or higher."" In simple terms, HSMS is hardware that protects private keys with built-in security mechanisms, and Gemini's HSMS provide premium-level security.&nbsp;</li><li>Third parties do annual penetration tests to assess potential weaknesses.</li><li>Gemini has a private Coordinated Disclosure Program for ethical hackers to report potential vulnerabilities.</li><li>Gemini has a community service for anyone to report fraudulent activity or scams.</li></ul><p>These are warp-level security measures and enable Gemini customers to feel safe that the platform is doing everything possible to protect their assets.&nbsp;</p><p><strong>Kraken also places security as high priority for its users, as per the the following: -</strong></p><ul><li>2FA withdrawal email confirmation</li><li>Air-gapped cold storage</li><li>Strict surveillance</li><li>Precise API key permission control</li><li>SSL encryption</li></ul><p>Overall, Kraken's high-level security is unquestionable and one of the reasons the platform has a high review rating. Kraken is one of the few major exchanges that have never experienced a security breach, they are ranked number 2 in the world behind <a href=""/review/crypto-com-review/"">Crypto.com</a> in terms of security by independent security company <a href=""https://cer.live/exchanges-rating/security"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Certified</a>, and have even launched <a href=""https://www.kraken.com/features/security/kraken-security-labs"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Kraken Security Labs</a>, a security company that works with other blockchain companies.</p><p>Both cryptocurrency exchanges offer exceptional levels of account security, so you can tick that as a top-tier bonus for both platforms.</p><h2>Gemini Overview</h2><h3>What is Gemini?</h3><p>Founded in 2014, Gemini is a privately-owned cryptocurrency exchange with a user-friendly platform that prioritises security and enables cryptocurrency users of all levels to easily buy, sell, trade, and safely store over 115 cryptocurrencies.</p><p>Notably, Gemini is majority-owned by Cameron and Tyler Winklevoss, who gained public attention through their legal battle against Mark Zuckerberg. The Winklevoss twins famously claimed that Facebook was their idea, resulting in a $65 million settlement. This incident led to the movie ""<a href=""https://www.imdb.com/title/tt1285016/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">The Social Network</a>."" Interestingly, all three were Harvard University students at the time.</p><p>The Gemini platform offers a tiered service catering to casual investors and hardcore traders, with separate interfaces and fee structures. It provides a user-friendly website and a beginner-friendly mobile app for on-the-go access.</p><p>Gemini has a good range of fiat currencies: -</p><ul><li>Australian Dollar (AUD)</li><li>Canadian Dollar (CAD)</li><li>Euro (EUR)</li><li>Great British Pound (GBP)&nbsp;</li><li>Hong Kong (HKD)</li><li>Singapore Dollar (SGD)</li><li>United States Dollar (USD)</li></ul><p>One distinctive feature of Gemini is its native currency, the Gemini dollar, which is a ""stablecoin"" pegged to the U.S. dollar, thus ensuring its value remains stable.</p><p>Gemini has gained popularity due to its emphasis on security and ease of use. It employs rigorous <a href=""/analysis/solving-blockchain-trilemma/"">security</a> measures, storing most users' cryptocurrencies in offline ""cold storage"" to protect against potential cyber threats.</p><p>Additionally, the exchange keeps ready funds in an insured ""hot wallet,"" ensuring quick access for users.</p><p>Over time, Gemini has evolved and introduced additional features to enhance its services. It now includes a payment app, an interest-paying savings account, a credit card, and a comprehensive trading platform.</p><p><a href=""https://coinmarketcap.com/rankings/exchanges/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">CoinMarketCap</a> lists Gemini within the top fifteen exchanges, with a <a href=""https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Volume_(finance)"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">trading volume</a> of over $10 million (24 hours) and 150 trading markets (May 2023).</p><blockquote><p>""The most trusted crypto-native finance platform. Create a free Gemini account in minutes."" (source: Gemini)</p></blockquote><p>The Gemini exchange quickly expanded internationally to Canada and the United Kingdom by mid-2016 and later to Hong Kong, Singapore, South Korea, and Japan to cater to the growing population of Asian cryptocurrency enthusiasts. Currently, Gemini operates in over 60 countries worldwide.</p><p>In September 2016, Gemini made crypto history by introducing the first-ever daily <a href=""/education/what-is-bitcoin/"">Bitcoin</a> auction. This innovative approach to trading quickly became standard practice in modern cryptocurrency exchanges, further establishing Gemini's influence in the industry.</p><p>Gemini is a reputable cryptocurrency with a comprehensive range of services, extensive cryptocurrency offerings, and a global presence, making it a popular choice among novice and experienced crypto enthusiasts.</p><h3>Cryptocurrencies Offered by Gemini</h3><p>Gemini offers more than 115 cryptocurrencies. That might not seem like a lot compared to other leading crypto platforms. However, Gemini aims to provide a range of cryptocurrencies established in the market, including the following: -</p><ul><li>Bitcoin (BTC)</li><li><a href=""https://cardano.org/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Cardano </a>(ADA)</li><li>Dogecoin (DOGE)</li><li>Ethereum (ETH)</li><li>Gemini Dollar (GUSD)</li><li>USD Coin (USDC)</li><li>Uniswap (UNI)&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li></ul><h3>Gemini Products</h3><p>Gemini has an impressive range of products for casual or advanced crypto traders and investors.</p><ul><li>ActiveTrader</li><li>Auction</li><li>Block Trade</li><li>Cryptopedia: Crypto Education</li><li>Gemini Credit Card (U.S. only)</li><li>Gemini Custody (crypto storage)</li><li>Gemini <a href=""/interview/market-protocol-ceo-seth-rubin/"">Derivatives</a></li><li>Gemini Dollar (native stablecoin)</li><li>Gemini Earn</li><li>Gemini Clearing</li><li>Gemini Mobile&nbsp;</li><li>Web Trader&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li></ul><blockquote><p>""Ask for permission, not for forgiveness. From day one, Gemini has prioritised the security of your assets. We never have and never will compromise on that."" (source: Gemini)</p></blockquote><h3>Gemini Types of Accounts and Fees</h3><p>When you open a Gemini Account, it has the following subaccounts:</p><blockquote><p>""One or more associated User Accounts; A fiat currency account (“Fiat Account”) that reflects its fiat currency balance; and A Digital Asset account (“Digital Asset Account”) that reflects its Digitals Asset balance. Each Digital Asset Account is subdivided into a depository account (“Depository Account) and a custody account (“Custody Account”)."" (source: Gemini)</p></blockquote><h3>Gemini Standard Account Fees</h3><ul><li>Less than $10.00 = $0.99</li><li>$10.00 to less than $25.00 = $1.49</li><li>$25.00 to less than $50.00 = $1.99</li><li>$50.00 to less than $200 = $2.99</li><li>$200+ = 1.49% of the order value&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li></ul><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/geminiawards_1fccd04ced.jpg"" alt=""geminiawards.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_geminiawards_1fccd04ced.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_geminiawards_1fccd04ced.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_geminiawards_1fccd04ced.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_geminiawards_1fccd04ced.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Gemini Has Won Many Awards: Image Source: Gemini</figcaption></figure><h3>Gemini Maker &amp; Taker Fees: Based on 30-Day Volume</h3><ul><li>0%: Maker 0.40% Taker 0.20%</li><li>$10,000 Maker 0.30% Taker 0.10%</li><li>$50,000 Maker 0.25% Taker 0.10%</li><li>$100,000 Maker 0.20% Taker 0.08%</li><li>$1,000,000 Maker 0.15% Taker 0.05%</li><li>$5,000,000 Maker 0.10% Taker 0.03%</li><li>$10,000,000 Maker 0.08% Taker 0.02%</li></ul><h3>Fiat Deposit Fees</h3><ul><li>ACH: Free</li><li>Wire Transfer: Free</li><li>Debit Card 3.49% of the total purchase amount</li><li>PayPal: 2.50% of the total deposit amount</li></ul><h3>Fiat Withdrawal Fees</h3><ul><li>ACH: Free</li><li>USD Wire Transfer: $25.00</li><li>Non-USD Bank Transfers: Free&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li></ul><h2>Gemini Security</h2><p>It is free to deposit cryptocurrencies to Gemini and transfer from Gemini Exchange to Gemini Custody. However, ""t<i>ransferring crypto from Gemini Custody to Gemini Exchange incurs a fee of $125 per withdrawal</i>.""</p><p>Gemini takes account security seriously and aims to protect against vulnerabilities with top-level measures, such as:&nbsp;</p><ul><li>2FA (Two-Factor Authentication).</li><li>Support for hardware security keys (Yubikey, for example).</li><li>Allowlisting (whitelisting) addresses.&nbsp;</li><li>Multisig (multiple signatures for transfers)</li><li>Rigorous employee background checks and ongoing screening.</li><li>All private keys are stored at high-security data centres offsite.&nbsp;</li><li>Production systems can only be accessed with hardware security keys (not susceptible to phishing).</li><li>Tyler Winklevoss (CEO) and Cameron Winklevoss (President) cannot jointly or individually transfer cryptocurrencies from the Gemini cold (offline) or hot (online) storage.</li></ul><p>&nbsp;</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/gemini_autotrader_bec300c427.jpg"" alt=""gemini_activetrader.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_gemini_autotrader_bec300c427.jpg 216w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_gemini_autotrader_bec300c427.jpg 500w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>High Performance Tools on Gemini For Active Traders: Image Source: Gemini</figcaption></figure><p>Overall, Gemini is a reputable cryptocurrency exchange with a good range of products and services suitable for advanced and novice users. Gemini focuses on providing top-level account security, which is a bonus for anyone considering opening a new account.</p><h2>Kraken Overview</h2><h3>What is Kraken?</h3><p>Kraken is the third-largest cryptocurrency exchange globally by volume and liquidity (<a href=""https://coinmarketcap.com/rankings/exchanges/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">CoinMarketCap</a>), with almost $300 million daily trading volume (24 hours) and more than 750 average liquidity (May 2023). <a href=""/review/kraken"">Kraken</a>, launched in 2011 and based in San Francisco, California, has over 700 markets and 225+ listed cryptocurrencies.</p><p><strong>Kraken supports a good range of fiat currencies: -</strong></p><ul><li>Australian Dollar (AUD)</li><li>Canadian Dollar (CAD)</li><li>Swiss Franc (CHF)&nbsp;</li><li>Euro (EUR)</li><li>Great British Pound (GBP)</li><li>Japanese Yen (JPY)</li><li>United States Dollar (USD)</li></ul><blockquote><p>""Kraken has the liquidity to fuel your business. Kraken is one of the longest-running, most trusted and healthiest exchanges. Our clients benefit from access to industry-leading liquidity, deep markets and direct access to our Principal OTC desk and Futures exchange"" (source: Kraken).</p></blockquote><p>Payward Inc owns Kraken, and in 2022, David Ripley replaced Jesse Powell as the CEO. An association with the leading market data provider helped Kraken gain popularity among the trader community.</p><p>Shortly afterwards, Kraken partnered with the popular chart service provider, <a href=""https://www.tradingview.com/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">TradingView</a>.</p><p>Cryptowatch is a unique Kraken portfolio management product where you can ""watch your portfolio and 2,000 crypto markets across multiple exchanges."" In addition, you can analyse the charts to monitor price movement, order flow, volume and more before trading on one of the multiple exchanges available and see real-time portfolio changes.</p><blockquote><p>""Cryptowatch makes it easy to keep tabs on the crypto markets and make trades when the conditions are right"" (source: Kraken).</p></blockquote><p>Kraken has an NFT marketplace and offers zero blockchain fees for <a href=""/education/fundamental-analysis-of-nfts/"">NFT </a>trading. You can track rarity scores, ""collect NFTs across multiple blockchains"", and bid with cash or crypto.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/kraken_staking_9c82f6d25a.jpg"" alt=""kraken_staking.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_kraken_staking_9c82f6d25a.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_kraken_staking_9c82f6d25a.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_kraken_staking_9c82f6d25a.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_kraken_staking_9c82f6d25a.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Earn A Yield By Staking Your Cryptos: Image Source: Kraken</figcaption></figure><h3>Cryptocurrencies Offered</h3><p>Kraken has a good range of top cryptocurrencies. Similarly to Gemini, Kraken lists cryptos with an established history, thus reducing the risks of onboarding potential scam coins or ponzi projects.</p><p><strong>The following are some of the top listed coins on Kraken: -</strong></p><ul><li><a href=""/education/what-is-bitcoin/"">Bitcoin </a>(BTC)</li><li>Bitcoin Cash (BCH)</li><li>Cardano (ADA)</li><li>Dogecoin (DOGE)</li><li><a href=""https://ethereum.org/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Ethereum </a>(ETH)</li><li>Litecoin (LTC)</li><li><a href=""https://polkadot.network/"" target=""_blank"" rel=""noopener"">Polkadot </a>(DOT)</li><li>USD Coin (USDC)</li></ul><p><strong>Kraken has a product range suitable for beginners and advanced traders and investors: -</strong></p><ul><li>Extensive Crypto Education</li><li>Kraken Mobile App</li><li>Kraken Pro Web &amp; Mobile Ap</li><li>Margin &amp; Futures Trading</li><li>An NFT Marketplace</li><li>Staking&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li></ul><blockquote><p>""Institutional clients enjoy fiat and crypto funding options with high monthly limits, including fiat funding in 7 global currencies, via multiple international partners. For the most efficient trade execution, we have expanded rate limits for clients trading algorithmically using either our REST or WebSocket APIs"" (source: Kraken)</p></blockquote><h3>Kraken Types of Accounts and Fees</h3><p><strong>Kraken provides three types of accounts: -</strong></p><ol style=""list-style-type:decimal;""><li>Starter</li><li>Intermediate&nbsp;</li><li>Pro</li></ol><p>Kraken has a strict KYC policy, and before trading or investing, your details require verification, such as a proof of address document, a valid government-issued I.D. document, a face photo, and an SSN (Social Security Number) or ITIN (Individual Taxpayer Identification Number).</p><p><strong>Kraken calculates maker and taker fees on a 30-day volume</strong></p><ul><li>$0 - $50,000: Maker 0.16% Taker 0.26%</li><li>$50,001 - $100,000: Maker 0.14% Taker 0.24%</li><li>$100,001 - $250,000: Maker 0.12% Taker 0.22%</li><li>$250,001 - $500,000: Maker 0.10% Taker 0.20%</li><li>$500,001 - $1,000,000: Maker 0.08% Taker 0.18%</li><li>$1,000,001 - $2,500,00: Maker 0.06% Taker 0.16%</li><li>$2,500,001 – $5,000,000: Maker 0.04% Taker 0.14%</li><li>$5,000,001 - $10,000,000: Maker 0.02% Taker 0.12%</li><li>$10,000,000+ Maker 0.00% Taker 0.10%</li></ul><h3>Fiat Deposit &amp; Withdrawal Fees</h3><p>Credit Card Deposits: 3.75% + €0.25 for each credit card purchase</p><p>ACH purchases vary</p><ul><li>There is a $10 minimum per transaction.</li><li>Six maximum transactions per 24 hours.</li><li>There is a $10,000 maximum spending within a time-based 7 day rolling period.</li><li>You can connect a maximum of three bank accounts at any given time.&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;</li></ul><p>For example, you can withdraw USD via Fedwire (USA only) with fees starting from $4.00 and worldwide via SWIFT from $13.00. Minimum withdrawal requirements depend on the method used and can take 1 – 5 days to deposit to your bank.</p><figure class=""image""><img src=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/kraken_institutions_09d503b5f1.jpg"" alt=""kraken_institutions.jpg"" srcset=""https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/thumbnail_kraken_institutions_09d503b5f1.jpg 245w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/small_kraken_institutions_09d503b5f1.jpg 500w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/medium_kraken_institutions_09d503b5f1.jpg 750w,https://image.coinbureau.dev/strapi/large_kraken_institutions_09d503b5f1.jpg 1000w,"" sizes=""100vw""><figcaption>Kraken Has The Liquidity To Fuel Your Business: Image Source: Kraken</figcaption></figure><h3>Kraken Security</h3><p>Kraken Security Labs has an ""<i>elite team of security researchers that aims to protect and grow the cryptocurrency ecosystem</i>."" (source: Kraken)</p><blockquote><p>""Kraken is the most secure digital asset exchange because we live and breathe security – in fact, we have multiple world-class teams dedicated to testing our products and services.
